findingпјү**пјҡз”ЁжҲ·й—®иҝҷдёӘ approved еҒҮи®ҫ OOS дёәдҪ• CAGR 100.76%/Sharpe 2.96/MDD вҲ’12.45%гҖӮзӣҙиҜ» run_dir `workspace/outputs/hypothesis_validation/lxr_v5_20260527_112442` зҡ„ IS/OOS diagnostics+event_driven_summary+report.csv+prescriptionгҖӮ**зЎ®еҮҝз»“и®әпјҲж— еҜ№еҶІпјү**пјҡв‘ **еҹәеҮҶжң¬иә«жҡҙж¶Ё**вҖ”вҖ”OOS зӘ—пјҲ2025-01-02вҶ’2026-02-27пјҢ277 ж—ҘпјүCSI500(000905.SH) иҮӘиә« **+51.2%**пјҲеј•ж“Һ bench ж—Ҙж”¶зӣҠеӨҚеҲ©е®һжөӢ 51.2%пјҢдёҺ summary дёҖиҮҙпјүпјҢзӯ–з•Ҙ beta 0.78 вҶ’ ~+40pp жҳҜзәҜеёӮеңә betaпјҲ"924"еҲәжҝҖ+2025 е°Ҹзӣҳ melt-up еҺҶеҸІжҖ§зүӣеёӮпјүгҖӮв‘Ў**"107% CAGR" жҳҜеҚ•дёӘ 13.5 жңҲзүӣзӘ—е№ҙеҢ–гҖҒйқһеҸҜжҢҒз»ӯзҺҮ**вҖ”вҖ”жҖ»ж”¶зӣҠ +123.3%/13.5 жңҲе№ҙеҢ–жҲҗ 107%пјӣ**еҗҢзӯ–з•Ҙ IS(2014-2024, 11y) еӨҚеҲ©д»… 20.5% CAGR**пјҲ5Г— дҪҺпјүгҖӮв‘ў**12% зҡ„ OOS еӣһж’ӨжҺ©зӣ–зңҹе®һ 49% еӣһж’ӨйЈҺйҷ©**вҖ”вҖ”еҗҢдёҖжң¬еӯҗ IS MDD **49.3%**пјҲ2015 еҙ©зӣҳвҶ’2018 зҶҠпјү/Sharpe **0.74**пјӣ2025 OOS зӘ—ж— жҢҒз»ӯзҶҠпјҲд»… 4 жңҲеҲқ 3 ж—Ҙе…ізЁҺи·Ң вҲ’12%пјүж•… Sharpe еҚ°жҲҗ 2.96гҖӮв‘Ј**и®ҫи®ЎжӯЈеҘҪеҺӢдёӯеҲ¶еәҰ**пјҡе°Ҹзӣҳ tilt(size lower-better)+иө„йҮ‘жөҒ+д»·еҖј+дҪҺжөҒеҠЁжҖ§жіўеҠЁ+еҸҚиҪ¬ = жӢҘжҢӨзҡ„е°ҸзӣҳеҠЁйҮҸ/иө„йҮ‘жөҒдәӨжҳ“пјҢжңҖеӨ§еҢ–еҗғ 2025 е°ҸзӣҳжҪ®пјӣIS-MDD-49% / OOS-MDD-12% дёҚеҜ№з§°еҚіжҢҮзә№гҖӮ**йқһжі„жјҸ**пјҡuniverse з”ҹеӯҳиҖ…е®үе…ЁпјҲall_market PIT еҗ«йҖҖеёӮгҖҒвүҘВҘ1bnгҖҒдёҠеёӮвүҘ250 ж—ҘпјүгҖҒж—¶й—ҙеҲҶеүІе№ІеҮҖпјҲISвүӨ2024-12-31 / OOS=еҶ»з»“ж—ҘеҺҶжңҖеҗҺ 14 жңҲзңҹе®һеүҚеҗ‘зӘ—пјүгҖҒеӣ еӯҗиө° sealed windowed-featuresгҖӮпјҲdiagnostics зҡ„ OOS rank_ic дёҺ IS еӯ—иҠӮзӣёеҗҢ 0.1488417136460393 = stub жңӘйҮҚз®— OOS IC зҡ„з‘•з–өпјҢдҪҶдёҚеҪұе“Қ event-driven еӣһжҠҘпјҢIS 20% vs OOS 107% зЎ®е®һдёҚеҗҢгҖӮпјү**е®Ўжү№жң¬иә«жҳҜ override**вҖ”вҖ”IS зЎ¬й—ё MDD 0.50/turnover 7.3 иў«и®°еҪ•еңЁжЎҲең°ж”ҫиЎҢпјҲжӯЈжҳҜзңӢжқҝ"вҡ и¶…1зЎ¬й—ё"ж Үи®°пјүгҖӮ**дёҺ [[strategy_v2_val_heavy_invalidated]]/[[research_long_only_50cagr]]/eps_diffusion еҗҢдёҖиҜҫ**пјҡиҝҮй—ё/approved вү  еҸҜйғЁзҪІеңЁиҜҘж”¶зӣҠзҺҮпјӣеҸҜйғЁзҪІзңҹзӣёжҳҜ through-cycle ISпјҲ~20% CAGR / Sharpe 0.74 / ~49% MDD / й«ҳжҚўжүӢпјүпјҢ100% жҳҜеҲ¶еәҰ+е№ҙеҢ–+иүҜжҖ§зӘ—дёүйҮҚж”ҫеӨ§зҡ„дә§зү©гҖӮи„ҡжң¬пјҡзӣҙиҜ»дёҠиҝ° run е·Ҙд»¶пјҲжңӘж”№д»»дҪ•з ”з©¶ж•°жҚ®пјүгҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **зңӢжқҝжӯЈејҸз ”з©¶жІ»зҗҶпјҡд»Һ"ж‘Ҡе№і5иЎЁ"йҮҚжһ„дёә"жҜҸеҒҮи®ҫдёҖжқЎж•…дәӢзәҝ"пјҲз”ЁжҲ·еҸҚйҰҲпјҡзјәдёҖзӣ®дәҶз„¶зҡ„"жөӢд»Җд№Ҳ/жҜҸжӯҘиҜҒе®һдәҶд»Җд№Ҳ/жңҖз»Ҳз»“и®ә"пјү**): з”ЁжҲ·жҢҮеҮәжҳЁеӨ©зҡ„жІ»зҗҶйЎөеҸӘжҳҜжҠҠжүҖжңүз ”з©¶зҡ„жҜҸдёҖжӯҘжҢүзұ»еһӢж‘Ҡе№ізҪ—еҲ—пјҲв‘  еҒҮи®ҫиЎЁ в‘Ў run иЎЁ в‘ў иЈҒеҶі в‘Ј е°Ғеӯҳ в‘Ө зҠ¶жҖҒеҸҳиҝҒпјүпјҢзңӢдёҚеҮәеҚ•дёӘ hypothesis еңЁжөӢд»Җд№ҲгҖҒжҜҸжӯҘиҜҒе®һдәҶд»Җд№ҲгҖҒжңҖз»Ҳе®һзҺ°дәҶд»Җд№ҲгҖӮ**йҮҚжһ„ [`governance.py`](src/dashboard/governance.py)+[`render.py`](src/dashboard/render.py)**пјҡжҠҠ в‘  ж”№жҲҗ**жҢүеҒҮи®ҫеҲҮзҡ„ж•…дәӢзәҝеҚЎ**пјҲ18 еј пјҢеҸҜеұ•ејҖпјүвҖ”вҖ”жҜҸеҚЎдёүж®өпјҡ**рҹҺҜ жөӢиҜ•д»Җд№Ҳ**пјҲи§Јжһҗ registration зҡ„ `hypothesis_json`пјҡthesis + mechanism + йў„жңҹж•Ҳеә” `expected_effect`пјҲstatistic/зӮ№дј°/CI/horizon/ж–№еҗ‘пјү+ **жҲҗеҠҹж ҮеҮҶ `success_criteria`**пјҲйў„е…ҲжүҝиҜәзҡ„й—ёпјҡrank_icirвүҘ/deflated_sharpeвүҘ/MDDвүӨ/turnoverвүӨ/corrвүӨпјү+ еӣ еӯҗ + universe/benchmark/rebalanceпјүпјӣ**рҹӘң жҜҸдёҖжӯҘиҜҒе®һдәҶд»Җд№Ҳ**пјҲж—¶й—ҙзәҝпјҡйў„жіЁеҶҢвҶ’еҗ„ gate_decisionпјҢжҜҸдёӘ gate жҠҠ `criteria_results_json` жёІжҲҗйҖҗжқЎ pass/fail иҚҜдёё `metric actual comp threshold вң“/вң—`пјҢе№¶йҷ„ `decision_reason`пјүпјӣ**рҹҸҒ жңҖз»Ҳз»“и®ә**пјҲз»ҲжҖҒ + зҗҶз”ұпјүгҖӮ**дёүжҖҒеҲӨе®ҡ**пјҲдҝ®дәҶдёҖдёӘдјҡиҜҜеҜјзҡ„зӮ№пјүпјҡcriteria зҡ„ `passed` жҳҜ True/False/None вҶ’ вң“йҖҡиҝҮ(з»ҝ)/вң—зЎ¬жҖ§жңӘиҝҮ(зәў, is_hard)/вң—иҪҜжҖ§жңӘиҫҫ(зҗҘзҸҖ)/вҖ“жңӘи®Ўз®—(зҒ°, еҰӮ `monotonicity_pvalue=None`)пјӣжҠҳеҸ ж‘ҳиҰҒдёҖиЎҢ `thesisвҖҰ вҶ’ з»ҲжҖҒпјҲжң«й—ё rank_icir еҖјпјү`гҖӮ**ж ёеҝғжІ»зҗҶдәӢе®һиў«жҳҫејҸжҡҙйңІ**пјҡ3 дёӘ approved еҒҮи®ҫе…¶е®һжҳҜ**еёҰзЎ¬й—ёжңӘиҝҮиў«и®°еҪ•еңЁжЎҲең°жү№еҮҶ**пјҲеҰӮ `hyp_20260527_lxr_005`пјҡis_only 5/8 йҖҡиҝҮеҗ« MDD 0.50>0.35гҖҒturnover 7.3>4.0 дёӨжқЎзЎ¬й—ёжңӘиҝҮпјҢoos_test еҸҲ 1 жқЎ turnover жңӘиҝҮпјҢ`decision_reason` еҶҷжҳҺ override зҗҶз”ұпјүвҶ’ жҠҳеҸ ж‘ҳиҰҒеҠ зәўиүІ **вҡ и¶…NзЎ¬й—ё** ж Үи®°пјҢдёҖзңјеҸҜи§Ғ"дёҚжҳҜе№ІеҮҖиҝҮй—ё"гҖӮв‘Ў в‘ў в‘Ј в‘Ө жҳҺз»ҶиЎЁжҠҳеҸ иҝӣ"в‘Ў еҺҹе§ӢжІ»зҗҶи®°еҪ•"еҸҜеұ•ејҖеқ—пјҲдҝқз•ҷеҸҜжҺ’еәҸпјүгҖӮйЎ¶йғЁеҠ иҚҜдёёеӣҫдҫӢгҖӮеҺҹе§Ӣж•°жҚ®е…ЁйғЁзңҹе®һпјҲDOM eval е®һжөӢпјҡ18 еҚЎгҖҒдёүж®өйҪҗе…ЁгҖҒ40 ж—¶й—ҙзәҝжӯҘгҖҒ66 з»ҝ+53 зәў+30 зҒ°иҚҜдёёгҖҒlxr_005 ж•…дәӢзәҝжӯЈзЎ®гҖҒoverride ж Үи®° 3 дёӘгҖҒna зҒ° rgb(110,118,129)гҖҒж—  console errorпјүгҖӮжһ„е»ә 0.8sгҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **зңӢжқҝз ”з©¶еұӮеҠ "жӯЈејҸз ”з©¶жІ»зҗҶ"еӯҗйЎөпјҲз”ЁжҲ·й—®"еҰӮдҪ•е®ҡд№ү/з•ҷжЎЈз ”з©¶гҖҒжңүж— жөҒзЁӢи§„иҢғ"пјү**): з”ЁжҲ·жҢҮеҮәзңӢжқҝз ”з©¶еұӮеҸӘжҠ•еҪұдәҶйқһжӯЈејҸ FINDINGS/йҮҢзЁӢзў‘пјҢжІЎеҸҚжҳ жӯЈејҸжІ»зҗҶгҖӮе…Ҳз”Ё Explore agent жҠҠз ”з©¶жІ»зҗҶж‘ёжё…пјҲжқғеЁҒжқҘжәҗпјүпјҡ**еҸ‘иө·дёҖж¬ЎжӯЈејҸз ”з©¶ = `hypothesis_cli.py register` йў„жіЁеҶҢдёҖдёӘ Hypothesis**пјҲеҶҷ `data/hypothesis_registry/hypothesis_events.parquet`пјҢ`design_hash` дёәиә«д»ҪгҖҒж”№жҺӘиҫһдёҚж”№иә«д»Ҫпјү+ и·‘ orchestrator runпјӣ**з•ҷжЎЈ**еӨҡеұӮ append-only жңәеҲ¶ејәеҲ¶вҖ”вҖ”run зӣ®еҪ•пјҲdag/steps/gate_reportпјүгҖҒ5 дёӘ registry зҡ„ master/evidence/`run_index`/`status_history`гҖҒ`testing_ledger`пјҲеӨҡйҮҚжЈҖйӘҢи®°иҙҰпјүгҖҒ`holdout_seals`пјҲOOS е°ҒеӯҳиҠұиҙ№гҖҒдёҚеҸҜйҮҚжөӢпјүгҖҒprovider_build й”ҡгҖҒproject_state еҸҷдәӢпјӣ**жөҒзЁӢи§„иҢғ**= `.agents/rules/research-integrity.md В§10`пјҲ10 йҳ¶ж®ө + 5 дәәй—ёпјү+ CLAUDE.md В§7/В§9 + factor_lifecycleгҖӮ**е®һзҺ°**пјҡж–°еўһ [`governance.py`](src/dashboard/governance.py) `collect_governance`пјҢз ”з©¶еұӮеҠ еӯҗеҜјиҲӘдёүйЎөпјҲйқһжӯЈејҸжҺўзҙў / жӯЈејҸз ”з©¶жІ»зҗҶ / йҮҢзЁӢзў‘пјүпјҢжІ»зҗҶйЎө 5 еј еҸҜжҺ’еәҸиЎЁвҖ”вҖ”в‘  йў„жіЁеҶҢеҒҮи®ҫ 18пјҲid/profile/зҠ¶жҖҒ/й—ёйҳ¶ж®ө/design/thesisпјүв‘Ў жӯЈејҸ run 25пјҲеҗ„ registry run_indexпјүв‘ў жөӢиҜ•иЈҒеҶіпјҲtesting_ledger 15 verdict/116 measurementпјүв‘Ј OOS е°ҒеӯҳиҠұиҙ№ 4пјҲholdout_sealsпјүв‘Ө зҠ¶жҖҒеҸҳиҝҒ 103пјҲstatus_historyпјүгҖӮDOM+жҲӘеӣҫе®һжөӢжёІжҹ“жӯЈзЎ®гҖӮиҜҡе®һзӮ№е·ІеҶҷиҝӣзңӢжқҝпјҡз ”з©¶еұӮжӯӨеүҚеҸӘжҳҫзӨәеҸҷдәӢеӯҗйӣҶпјҢзҺ°иЎҘдёҠжӯЈејҸжІ»зҗҶйқўгҖӮжһ„е»ә 0.8sпјӣеҢ…еҶ… 13 жЁЎеқ—пјҲ+governance.pyпјүгҖӮMLflow д»ҚжҳҜзјәеҸЈпјҲВ§7 иҰҒжұӮдҪҶ mlruns иҝ‘з©әпјүгҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **зңӢжқҝзҝ»иҜ‘иЎҘиҜ‘еҒҡжҲҗ"дјҡиҜқеҶ…дёҖй”®"`/backfill-translations`пјӣheadless `claude -p` иҮӘеҠЁеҢ–жӯӨжңәдёҚеҸҜиЎҢпјҲе®һжөӢ 401пјҢи®°еҪ•д»Ҙе…ҚйҮҚжҹҘпјү**): з”ЁжҲ·жғіжҠҠ"ж–°еӣ еӯҗзјәдёӯиӢұж–ҮжҸҸиҝ°"зҡ„иЎҘиҜ‘иҮӘеҠЁеҢ–гҖҒдё”ж—  Anthropic API keyпјҲеҸӘиғҪиө° Claude и®ўйҳ…пјүгҖӮ**ж·ұжҹҘ headless `claude -p`пјҲB ж–№жЎҲпјүз»“и®әпјҡжӯӨжңәдёҚеҸҜиЎҢ**вҖ”вҖ”CLI еңЁпјҲ`claude.exe` v2.1.169пјҢеҸҜиў«и®ЎеҲ’д»»еҠЎи°ғз”ЁпјүпјҢжӯЈзЎ®зҡ„жңҖе°Ҹжқғйҷҗж Үеҝ—д№ҹзЎ®и®ӨеӯҳеңЁпјҲ`--permission-mode dontAsk` иҮӘеҠЁжӢ’йқһзҷҪеҗҚеҚ•е·Ҙе…·гҖҒ`--allowedTools "Read(..)" "Write(..)"` ж–Үд»¶зә§йҷҗе®ҡгҖҒ`--model sonnet`гҖҒ`--max-budget-usd`гҖҒ`--bare` и·ій’©еӯҗгҖҒ`-p` й…Қ `< /dev/null` йҳІ stdin еҚЎпјүпјҢжңәеҲ¶иғҪи·‘еҮә JSONвҖ”вҖ”**дҪҶи®ӨиҜҒ 401**пјҡжң¬жңә Claude и®ӨиҜҒжҳҜе®ҝдё»/зҪ‘е…ід»ЈзҗҶзҡ„пјҲenv жңү `ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL`+`CLAUDE_CODE_SDK_HAS_HOST_AUTH_REFRESH=1`пјүпјҢspawn зҡ„ж— еӨҙиҝӣзЁӢжӢҝдёҚеҲ°иҜҘи®ӨиҜҒпјҢеҚ•еҮӯ `.credentials.json` и®ўйҳ… token д№ҹжІЎи®ӨиҜҒжҲҗпјҲжҠҠзҪ‘е…і/дјҡиҜқ env unset еҗҺд»Қ 401пјүгҖӮж— дәәеҖје®ҲиҰҒеҸҜиЎҢйЎ» `claude setup-token`пјҲдәӨдә’гҖҒд»…з”ЁжҲ·иғҪеҒҡпјү+ иҗҪзӣҳй•ҝжңҹ token + иҮӘдё» agentвҖ”вҖ”дҪҺйў‘д»»еҠЎдёҚеҲ’з®—гҖӮ**ж•…йҮҮз”Ё"дјҡиҜқеҶ…дёҖй”®"**пјҡж–°еўһ [`backfill_translations.py`](src/dashboard/backfill_translations.py)пјҲ`detect` жүҫзјәеҸЈеҶҷ `_backfill_input.json` / `merge` ж ЎйӘҢеҗҲе№¶ `_backfill_output.json`вҶ’`translations.json` е№¶жё…зҗҶпјҢзЎ®е®ҡжҖ§ Pythonпјү+ ж–ңжқ е‘Ҫд»Ө [`/backfill-translations`](.claude/commands/backfill-translations.md)пјҲи®©еҪ“еүҚдјҡиҜқзҡ„ Sonnet и·‘е®Ң detectвҶ’иҜ‘вҶ’mergeвҶ’йҮҚе»әпјүгҖӮ**е®һжөӢе…ЁжөҒзЁӢ**пјҡеҲ  `tech_rsi_14`вҶ’detect жүҫеҲ° 1вҶ’еҶҷиҜ‘ж–ҮвҶ’merge иҝҳеҺҹвҶ’detect жҠҘ"ж— йңҖиЎҘиҜ‘"вҶ’йҮҚе»әеҗҺ рҹ©ә зҝ»иҜ‘иҰҶзӣ– 185/185гҖӮйӣ¶ key/token/ж— дәәеҖје®Ҳ agentгҖӮеүҜеҸ‘зҺ°пјҡж— еӨҙдјҡиҜқз»“жқҹдјҡи§ҰеҸ‘жҲ‘зҡ„ SessionEnd й’©еӯҗпјҢWindows и·Ҝеҫ„еңЁ bash дёӢиў«жү“ж•ЈпјҲ`--bare` еҸҜи§„йҒҝпјүгҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **зңӢжқҝиҮӘе®Ўжәҗж–Үд»¶ж–°йІңеәҰ/дёҖиҮҙжҖ§пјҲз”ЁжҲ·й—®"еҰӮдҪ•дҝқйҡңдҫқиө–ж–Үд»¶йҡҸйЎ№зӣ®е®һж—¶жӣҙж–°"пјү+ еӣ еӯҗиЎЁжҺ’еәҸ + дјҡиҜқеҺ»йҮҚ + йЎөйқўиҮӘеҠЁеҲ·ж–°**): дёүжү№е°Ҹиҝӯд»ЈгҖӮ**(1) жәҗж–Үд»¶ж–°йІңеәҰиҮӘе®Ў**вҖ”вҖ”ж ёеҝғи®ӨзҹҘпјҡзңӢжқҝеҸӘиғҪеҝ е®һеҸҚжҳ жәҗж–Үд»¶гҖҒж— жі•дҝқиҜҒжәҗж–Үд»¶иҮӘиә«ж–°йІңпјҲAзұ»йҡҸжІ»зҗҶ gate иҮӘеҠЁжӣҙж–°еҰӮ registry/field_status/git/transcriptпјӣBзұ»йқ зәӘеҫӢеҰӮ project_state/FINDINGS/board.yamlпјӣCзұ»зј“еӯҳеҰӮ translations.jsonпјүгҖӮи§Јжі•жҳҜи®©зңӢжқҝ**иҮӘжЈҖе№¶ж ҮзәўиҗҪеҗҺ**пјҡж–°еўһ [`health.py`](src/dashboard/health.py) `collect_health`пјҢиҗҪең°йЎөйЎ¶йғЁ"рҹ©ә ж•°жҚ®ж–°йІңеәҰ/дёҖиҮҙжҖ§иҮӘе®Ў"йқўжқҝпјҢжҜҸж¬ЎйҮҚе»әи·‘ 5 жЈҖжҹҘвҖ”вҖ”в‘  catalogпјҲ`catalog_composition()` д»Јз Ғе®һж—¶пјүvs registry еҪ“еүҚж•°пјҲдёҚдёҖиҮҙвҶ’йңҖ sync_catalogпјүв‘Ў Sonnet зҝ»иҜ‘иҰҶзӣ–зјәеҸЈ в‘ў project_state йЎ¶йғЁ Update Note ж—Ҙжңҹ vs жңҖж–° commit ж—ҘжңҹпјҲиҗҪеҗҺвҶ’иЎҘи®°еҪ•пјүв‘Ј жңҖиҝ‘ `run_daily_qa` йҖҡиҝҮзҺҮ+ж—¶ж•ҲпјҲиҜ» `logs/qa_report_*.json` зҡ„ `checks[].ok`пјүв‘Ө 6 дёӘе…ій”®жәҗж–Үд»¶ mtime дёҖи§ҲгҖӮд»»дёҖ warnвҶ’йқўжқҝиҪ¬зҗҘзҸҖгҖӮе®һжөӢеҪ“еүҚ 3 ok+1 warnпјҲQA 2 еӨ©еүҚ 8/10пјҢжӯЈзЎ®жҡҙйңІпјүгҖӮ**(2) еӣ еӯҗиЎЁиЎЁеӨҙзӮ№еҮ»жҺ’еәҸ**пјҲgeneric JSпјҢж•ҙж јеҲӨж•°еҖј/еӯ—з¬ҰдёІвҖ”вҖ”`earn_..._60` дёҚиҜҜеҲӨдёәж•°еӯ—пјӣOSAP/дҝЎеҸ·иЎЁеҗҢдә«пјүгҖӮ**(3) дјҡиҜқеҗҢж ҮйўҳеҺ»йҮҚ**пјҡ67 transcript йҮҢ 0 зңҹйҮҚеӨҚ idпјҢдҪҶеҫҲеӨҡ session еҗҢејҖеңәзҷҪпјҲйҮҚеҸ‘/з»ӯжҺҘпјүвҶ’ жҢүжҙҫз”ҹж ҮйўҳеҗҲе№¶дҝқз•ҷжңҖиҝ‘дёҖжқЎ+`Г—N` и§’ж ҮпјҲ67вҶ’29пјүгҖӮ**(4) йЎөйқўиҮӘеҠЁеҲ·ж–°**пјҡжһ„е»әеҶҷж № `build_id.txt`пјҲgitignoreпјүпјҢйЎөйқўжҜҸ 30s иҪ®иҜўжҜ”еҜ№зғҳз„ҷзҡ„ `BUILD_ID`вҖ”вҖ”еҗҺеҸ°/з©әй—Іж ҮзӯҫйЎөйқҷй»ҳ reloadгҖҒжҙ»еҠЁж ҮзӯҫйЎөеј№"зӮ№еҮ»еҲ·ж–°"е°ҸжқЎпјҲе®һжөӢз©әй—ІйЎөиҮӘе·ұ reload жҲҗеҠҹпјүгҖӮе…ЁйғЁ DOM eval йӘҢиҜҒгҖӮжһ„е»ә 0.7sгҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **зңӢжқҝ md йЎөеҶ…жҹҘзңӢе…ҚжүӢеҠЁпјҡеёёй©»жң¬ең°жңҚеҠЎпјҲat-logon и®ЎеҲ’д»»еҠЎпјү**): з”ЁжҲ·дёҚжғіжҜҸж¬ЎжүӢеҠЁеҸҢеҮ» `serve_dashboard.bat`гҖӮи§Јжі•пјҡж–°еўһ **at-logon и®ЎеҲ’д»»еҠЎ `QuantDashboardServe`** з”Ё pythonw еҗҺеҸ°еёёй©»дёҖдёӘз»‘ `127.0.0.1:8799` зҡ„йқҷй»ҳ http жңҚеҠЎпјҢејҖжңәиҮӘеҠЁиө· вҶ’ зңӢжқҝж°ёиҝңеңЁ `http://127.0.0.1:8799/` еҸҜз”ЁпјҢmd йЎөеҶ…жҹҘзңӢдёҖзӣҙз”ҹж•ҲпјҢйӣ¶жүӢеҠЁгҖӮ**иё©дәҶдёӨдёӘзңҹеқ‘**пјҡ(a) `Register-ScheduledTask` зҡ„ `-AtLogOn` й»ҳи®Өе…Ёз”ЁжҲ·и§ҰеҸ‘еҷЁвҶ’йңҖз®ЎзҗҶе‘ҳвҶ’"Access denied"пјӣз»ҷи§ҰеҸ‘еҷЁеҠ  `-User <еҪ“еүҚз”ЁжҲ·>` йҷҗе®ҡеҚіе…ҚжҸҗжқғгҖӮ(b) **stock `python -m http.server` еңЁ pythonwпјҲж— зӘ—еҸЈпјүдёӢжҜҸдёӘиҜ·жұӮйғҪиҝ”еӣһз©әе“Қеә”пјҲHTTP 000пјү**вҖ”вҖ”еӣ дёәе®ғжҠҠиҜ·жұӮж—Ҙеҝ—еҶҷ stderrпјҢpythonw жІЎжңү stderr дјҡжҠӣй”ҷпјӣж•…ж–°еўһйқҷй»ҳжңҚеҠЎи„ҡжң¬ [`serve.py`](src/dashboard/serve.py)пјҲ`log_message` зҪ®з©ә + `directory=ROOT`пјүпјҢpythonw и·‘е®ғ curl е®һжөӢ index/md еқҮ **HTTP 200**гҖӮNB жң¬жңә venv зҡ„ pythonw жҳҜйҮҚе®ҡеҗ‘еҷЁпјҲдјҡеҶҚ exec еҹәзЎҖ `C:\ProgramData\anaconda3\pythonw.exe`пјҢеҸҢиҝӣзЁӢпјүпјҢд»»еҠЎзӣҙжҺҘз”Ё anaconda pythonwпјҲеҚ•иҝӣзЁӢгҖҒstdlib и¶іеӨҹпјүгҖӮж–°еўһ [`open_dashboard.bat`](src/dashboard/open_dashboard.bat)пјҲдёҖй”®ејҖжөҸи§ҲеҷЁеҲ°иҜҘең°еқҖпјҢжҲ–зӣҙжҺҘж”¶и—Ҹ URLпјүпјӣ`serve_dashboard.bat` йҷҚдёәжүӢеҠЁеӨҮз”ЁгҖӮе®үе…Ёпјҡд»… 127.0.0.1пјҢhttp.server ж—  CORS еӨҙвҶ’и·ЁжәҗиҜ»дёҚеҲ°гҖӮдёүи®ЎеҲ’д»»еҠЎе№¶еӯҳпјҡ`QuantDashboardRefresh`пјҲжҜҸе°Ҹж—¶йҮҚе»әпјү+ `QuantDashboardServe`пјҲеёёй©»жңҚеҠЎпјү+ SessionEnd й’©еӯҗпјҲз»“жқҹйҮҚе»әпјүгҖӮйӘҢиҜҒпјҡд»»еҠЎ trigger=LogonгҖҒState=RunningгҖҒserving HTTP 200гҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **зңӢжқҝдәӨдә’еҚҮзә§пјҲз”ЁжҲ·жҢҮзӨәпјүпјҡзӯӣйҖүеҷЁ + ж•°жҚ®еӯҗеҜјиҲӘ + еӣ еӯҗдё»д»Һ + md йЎөеҶ…жҹҘзңӢ + дјҡиҜқд»»еҠЎжӢҶеҲҶ**): жҢүз”ЁжҲ· 5 йЎ№иҰҒжұӮеҠ еүҚз«ҜдәӨдә’пјҲзәҜ JSпјҢдёҚзў°ж•°жҚ®пјүгҖӮ(1) **ж•°жҚ®еұӮгҖҢе…ЁйғЁж•°жҚ®йӣҶгҖҚеҠ жҢүзҠ¶жҖҒзӯӣйҖүжқЎ**пјҲapproved/quarantine/rawвҖҰ+ж–Үжң¬пјүпјҢзҠ¶жҖҒжҳҫи‘— pillгҖӮ(2) **Qlib universe еҚҮдёәдёҺе…ЁйғЁж•°жҚ®йӣҶеҗҢзә§зҡ„еӯҗйЎө**вҖ”вҖ”ж•°жҚ®еұӮеҶ…еҠ еӯҗеҜјиҲӘ `е…ЁйғЁж•°жҚ®йӣҶв”ғQlib universeв”ғеӯ—ж®өдҝғиҝӣ`пјҢuniverse еҚ•зӢ¬жҲҗйЎөпјҲиЎЁ+ж Үзҡ„ж•°+ж—ҘеҺҶпјүпјҢдёҚеҶҚжҳҜи§’иҗҪе°ҸеҚЎгҖӮ(3) **еӣ еӯҗеұӮеҠ зӯӣйҖүжқЎпјҲзҠ¶жҖҒ/зұ»еҲ«/ж–Үжң¬пјү+ ж”№дё»д»ҺејҸ**пјҡжұҮжҖ»иЎЁжҳҜдё»еҲ—иЎЁпјҢзӮ№иЎҢе°ұең°еұ•ејҖиҜҘеӣ еӯҗжҳҺз»ҶеҚЎпјҢеҲ жҺүе№ій“әзҡ„ 185 еҚЎпјҲйЎәеёҰйЎөйқўеҸҳиҪ»гҖҒжҲӘеӣҫе·Ҙе…·еҸҲиғҪз”ЁдәҶпјүгҖӮ(4) **md ж–ҮжЎЈй“ҫжҺҘйЎөеҶ…жҹҘзңӢ**пјҡзӮ№ `.md` еј№йЎөеҶ…жЁЎжҖҒз”ЁеҶ…зҪ®жһҒз®Җ mdвҶ’html жёІжҹ“пјҢдёҚи·іеҮәпјӣз”Ё `fetch` ж•… file:// еҸҢеҮ»дёҚеҸҜз”Ё вҶ’ ж–°еўһ [`serve_dashboard.bat`](src/dashboard/serve_dashboard.bat)пјҲз»‘ 127.0.0.1 иө· http.server + ејҖжөҸи§ҲеҷЁпјүпјҢfile:// дёӢжЁЎжҖҒз»ҷжҸҗзӨә+зӣҙејҖй“ҫжҺҘпјӣ`*_review.html`/еӨ–й“ҫз…§еёёгҖӮ(5) **дјҡиҜқйЎө**пјҡжҙҫз”ҹзІҫз®Җж Үйўҳ + жҠҠ **Task-tool д»»еҠЎ**пјҲ`~/.claude/tasks/<sid>/`пјҢsessions.py ж–°еўһ `_session_tasks` жҜҸж¬ЎеҲ·ж–°иҜ»еҸ–гҖҒдёҚе…Ҙзј“еӯҳпјү/TodoWrite жӢҶжҲҗ **вң…е·Іе®ҢжҲҗ/рҹ”өиҝӣиЎҢдёӯ**пјҲеӨҙйғЁи®Ўж•°+еұ•ејҖжҳҺз»Ҷпјүпјӣжң¬зҺҜеўғ 67 дјҡиҜқдёӯд»… 16 з”ЁиҝҮ Task е·Ҙе…·гҖҒжҳҫзӨәдёӯзҡ„ 4 дёӘжңүд»»еҠЎпјҢе…¶дҪҷд»Ҙ commit/ж–Үд»¶/ж‘ҳиҰҒдҪ“зҺ°гҖӮ**дҝ®дәҶдёҖдёӘзңҹ bug**пјҡж•°жҚ®еӯҗйЎөжјҸй—ӯеҗҲ `</div>` иҮҙ uni/appr еөҢиҝӣ setsпјҲйҡҗи—ҸпјүпјҢиЎҘй—ӯеҗҲгҖӮе…ЁзЁӢ DOM eval йӘҢиҜҒпјҲдё»д»Һ 185 иЎҢ 0 е№ій“әеҚЎгҖҒеӯҗеҜјиҲӘеҲҮжҚўгҖҒеӣ еӯҗзӯӣйҖү approvedвҶ’8гҖҒ22 дёӘ md жЁЎжҖҒй“ҫжҺҘгҖҒmd fetch 200гҖҒдјҡиҜқ 4 дёӘжңү вң…/рҹ”өгҖҒuniverse 6 иЎҢпјүгҖӮжһ„е»ә 0.7s вҶ’ 826KBгҖӮREADMEгҖҢдәӨдә’гҖҚиҠӮе·ІеҠ гҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-09, **дёӯеҝғеҢ–зңӢжқҝеҜҢеҢ–йҮҚжһ„ + е…ЁйғЁзҝ»иҜ‘иө° Claude SonnetпјҲз”ЁжҲ·жҢҮзӨәпјү**): жҢүз”ЁжҲ·иҰҒжұӮжҠҠзңӢжқҝд»Һ"з®Җз•Ҙж‘ҳиҰҒ"еҚҮзә§дёә"йҖҗеұӮжҳҺз»ҶйЎө"пјҢе№¶жҠҠжүҖжңүеҸҢиҜӯжҸҸиҝ°ж”№з”ұ **Claude Sonnet з”ҹжҲҗ**пјҲеҸ–д»ЈжүӢеҶҷиҜҚиЎЁпјүгҖӮ**еёғеұҖ**пјҡеҲ йҷӨйЎ¶йғЁе…ЁеұҖ KPI еӨ§еҚЎеёҰпјҢжҜҸеұӮйЎөйҰ–иҮӘеёҰ lead еҚЎгҖӮ**зҹҘиҜҶеұӮ**пјҡOSAP еӯҰжңҜеӣ еӯҗ 212 жқЎ AиӮЎдёүзӯӣиЎЁпјҲfeasibility/novelty ж ҮзӯҫгҖҒUS t-statгҖҒour_prefixгҖҒdup_matchпјү+ arXiv q-fin 80 зҜҮпјҲеҸҜеұ•ејҖж‘ҳиҰҒпјү+ иҒҡе®Ҫ strategy_kb/еӣһжөӢжҳҺз»Ҷ + temp_plan иҜҠж–ӯ + и®°еҝҶгҖӮ**ж•°жҚ®еұӮ**пјҡ35 ж•°жҚ®йӣҶ Г— **661 еҲ—йҖҗеҲ—дёӯиӢұж–Ү**пјҲи§Јжһҗ `data_dictionary.md`пјҢжң¬е°ұеҸҢиҜӯпјҢж–°жЁЎеқ— `dictionary.py`пјүеҸҜеұ•ејҖпјҢзҠ¶жҖҒ raw/approved/quarantine + жҳҜеҗҰе…Ҙ QlibгҖӮ**еӣ еӯҗеұӮ**пјҡ185 дёӘеӣ еӯҗжҳҺз»ҶеҚЎпјҲreview.html еҜ№йҪҗпјҡзҠ¶жҖҒ/жҺЁиҚҗ/зұ»еҲ«/kind/ж–№еҗ‘/иЎЁиҫҫејҸ/жҲҗеҲҶ/иҜҒжҚ® chipsпјү+ жұҮжҖ»еӨ§иЎЁ + зұ»еҲ«еҲҶеёғжқЎгҖӮ**з ”з©¶/зӯ–з•ҘеұӮ**пјҡз ”з©¶зәҝзЁӢеҗ« FINDINGS ж‘ҳиҰҒгҖҒйҮҢзЁӢзў‘ж—¶й—ҙзәҝпјӣ372 дҝЎеҸ·иЎЁ + еҸҜйғЁзҪІд№ҰгҖӮ**зҝ»иҜ‘жңәеҲ¶**пјҡеӣ еӯҗ/зұ»зӣ®/зӯ–з•Ҙ/зәҝзЁӢзҡ„дёӯиӢұж–ҮдёҖеҸҘиҜқжҸҸиҝ°е…ЁйғЁ Sonnet з”ҹжҲҗ вҶ’ зј“еӯҳ `src/dashboard/translations.json`пјҲcommittedпјҢ185 еӣ еӯҗ+17 зұ»зӣ®+2 зӯ–з•Ҙ+16 зәҝзЁӢпјҢйӣ¶зјәеӨұпјүпјӣж–°жЁЎеқ— `translate.py` жһ„е»әж—¶еҸӘиҜ»зј“еӯҳпјҲеҝ«/зҰ»зәҝ/е…Қ API keyпјҢе‘ҪдёӯдёҚеҲ°вҶ’з©әдёІдёҚжҠҘй”ҷпјүпјӣж•°жҚ®еұӮдёҚиө° SonnetпјҲеӯ—е…ёжң¬е°ұеҸҢиҜӯпјүгҖӮеҲ йҷӨејғз”Ёзҡ„ `gloss.py`гҖӮ**иё©еқ‘+и§Јжі•пјҲе·Іеӯҳи®°еҝҶ [[feedback_redundant_agents_for_flaky_network]]пјү**пјҡSonnet еӯҗд»ЈзҗҶзҪ‘з»ңжһҒдёҚзЁіпјҲECONNRESET/socketпјҢ~50%/ж¬ЎеӨұиҙҘпјүпјҢйқ **е№¶еҸ‘еӨҡеҸ‘еҶ—дҪҷ agent + и®©е…¶иҝ”еӣһ JSON дёҚеҶҷж–Үд»¶ + йғЁеҲҶжҲҗеҠҹз«ӢеҚіиҗҪзӣҳ + еҲҶжү№**жҠўжҲҗеҠҹпјҲ185вҶ’2Г—93пјүгҖӮжһ„е»ә 0.6s вҶ’ ж № `index.html` 808KBпјӣDOM eval йӘҢиҜҒе…ЁйғЁжёІжҹ“жӯЈзЎ®пјҲ185 еҚЎ/35 йӣҶ/212 OSAP/80 arXiv/ж— йЎ¶йғЁеҚЎеёҰпјүпјҢд»… preview жҲӘеӣҫе·Ҙе…·еҗғдёҚдёӢиҝҷд№ҲеӨ§зҡ„йЎөпјҲйқһзјәйҷ·пјҢжөҸи§ҲеҷЁзӣҙејҖжӯЈеёёпјүгҖӮи®ҫи®Ўи§Ғ [src/dashboard/README.md](src/dashboard/README.md)гҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-09, **Part B (pit_* parity-validated vs vendor q_*) + Part C (3 PIT single-quarter margin factors added)** вҖ” follow-on to the indicators rebuild): **Part B** вҖ” validated our self-computed `pit_*` single-quarter YoY against Tushare's independent vendor `q_*` (recompute via the DEPLOYED `derive_single_quarter_value`+`percent_change`+`same_period_last_year_end` on the income ledger vs the raw indicators ledger's `q_netprofit_yoy`/`q_op_yoy`/`q_sales_yoy`; 253,692 firm-quarters). Result: **~90% near-exact** (|О”|<0.05pp), Spearman 0.97-0.98, sign-agreement 99%, **Pearson 0.95-0.99 after clipping |YoY|>300%** вҖ” the raw Pearson near-0 (netprofit/sales) was PURELY ~1.5-3% extreme near-zero-base YoY blow-ups (our `percent_change` and the vendor clamp them differently; mathematical YoY-ratio instability, NOT a core-computation bug). **Verdict: our pit_* is correct/trustworthy** (growth factors should winsorize, as the library already does). Report [PIT_VS_VENDOR_Q_PARITY.md](workspace/research/data_audit/PIT_VS_VENDOR_Q_PARITY.md); script `workspace/scripts/validate_pit_vs_vendor_q.py` (pure pandas + deployed primitives, no qlib/loader/find/du). **Part C** вҖ” added 3 PIT single-quarter MARGIN factors to the catalog: `qual_q_net_margin` = `Ref($n_income_attr_p_sq_q0,1)/Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)`, `qual_q_gross_margin` = `(Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)-Ref($oper_cost_sq_q0,1))/Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)`, `qual_q_op_margin` = `Ref($operate_profit_sq_q0,1)/Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)` вҖ” the PIT-correct alternative to Tushare's vendor `q_netprofit_margin`/`q_gsprofit_margin`, built on the Part-B-validated single-quarter `_sq_q0` derivation. All fields field-approved (income `_sq` family); PIT-safe (every `$field` `Ref(...,1)`-wrapped). `catalog_composition().total` вҶ’185 (DERIVED, not pinned); synced to `factor_master` as **draft** (parity_ok, +3 rows). Tests: PIT-safety + `TestFormalFactorCompatibility` + `test_factor_registry` PASS. Expense-ratio / `*_to_ebt` single-quarter ratios DEFERRED (need `sell_exp_sq_q0`/`admin_exp_sq_q0`/`total_profit_sq_q0` approved first). These are `draft` factors вҖ” candidate/approved promotion is a separate gated step. Memory: [[project_field_parity_audit_2026_06_08]].*

*Update Note (2026-06-09, **EventDrivenBacktester йҖҖеёӮ/еҒңзүҢеҒҘеЈ®жҖ§дёӨеӨ„дҝ®еӨҚпјҲз”ЁжҲ·жҢҮзӨәпјү**): дҝ®дәҶ event-driven еј•ж“ҺйҮҢдёӨдёӘдёҺ"еҒңзүҢвҶ’NaN д»·ж ј"зӣёе…ізҡ„еҒҘеЈ®жҖ§зјәйҷ·гҖӮ**(1) зӯ–з•ҘдёӢеҚ• NaN еҙ©жәғпјҲеҺҹе§Ӣд»»еҠЎпјү**пјҡ`RankedFallbackStrategy` иө°зҡ„е…ұдә«дёӢеҚ•еҮҪж•° [strategies.py `_emit_rebalance_orders`](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/strategies.py) еңЁ trim еҲҶж”Ҝз”Ё `int(max(diff,0)/ref_price/lot)*lot`пјҢеҪ“дёҖдёӘ**жҢҒд»“**еҪ“ж—ҘеҒңзүҢж—¶ `prev_day` ж”¶зӣҳдёә NaN вҶ’ `ref_price=NaN`пјҲ`NaN<=0` дёә FalseпјҢж—§ `<=0` е®ҲеҚ«жјҸиҝҮпјүвҶ’ `int(NaN)` жҠӣ `ValueError: cannot convert float NaN to integer`пјҢж•ҙдёӘеӣһжөӢеҙ©пјҲtopk=50 ж—¶дёҖеҸӘеҲҶжһҗеёҲиҰҶзӣ–зҘЁдёӯйҖ”еҒңзүҢи§ҰеҸ‘пјӣtopk=30 дёҚи§ҰеҸ‘пјүгҖӮдҝ®еӨҚпјҡе®ҲеҚ«ж”№ `pd.isna(ref_price) or ref_price<=0` вҶ’ и·іиҝҮ trimгҖҒжҠҠд»“дҪҚз»“иҪ¬еҲ°дёӢж¬Ўи°ғд»“пјҲеҒңзүҢзҘЁжң¬е°ұдёҚеҸҜи°ғпјӣеј•ж“ҺеҸҰжңү vol==0 д»ЈзҗҶеңЁжҲҗдәӨеұӮ blockпјүгҖӮд№°е…ҘеҲҶж”Ҝж—  `int()`гҖҒ`max(NaN,вҖҰ)`/`NaN>1.0` дёҚжҠӣ вҶ’ е·ІиҮӘз„¶з»“иҪ¬пјҢдёҚеҠЁгҖӮ**(2) йҖҖеёӮ force-close еӣһйҖҖеҠ еӣә**пјҡе…Ҳз”Ёзңҹе®һж•°жҚ®жҹҘжё…жңәеҲ¶вҖ”вҖ”йҖҖеёӮдёҺеҒңзүҢз”ұ **PIT universe иҫ№з•Ң**пјҲ`all_stocks.txt`пјҢ`get_index_constituents('all')`вҶ’`D.list_instruments`пјүиҮӘз„¶еҢәеҲҶпјҡеҒңзүҢзҘЁд»ҚеңЁ universe вҶ’ `D.features` иҝ”еӣһ **NaN иЎҢ**пјҲе®һжөӢ 2023-06-15пјҡ5242 еңЁеҶҢе…ЁйғЁиҝ”еӣһгҖҒ0 зјәиЎҢгҖҒ57 еҸӘеҒңзүҢзҘЁ vol/close/open е…Ё NaNпјүвҶ’ еңЁ `today_codes` йҮҢ вҶ’ **дёҚ force-closeгҖҒз»“иҪ¬**пјӣйҖҖеёӮзҘЁйҖҖеҮә universe вҶ’ ж— иЎҢ вҶ’ `_handle_delistings`пјҲ[engine.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/engine.py) `BacktestEngine` ж–№жі•пјҢжҜҸдәӨжҳ“ж—ҘејҖзӣҳеүҚи·‘пјүforce-closeгҖӮ**е…ій”®дәӢе®һпјҲеҶіе®ҡдёҚеҠ  haircutпјү**пјҡйҖҖеёӮеүҚзҡ„йҖҖеёӮж•ҙзҗҶжңҹжҡҙи·Ң**е·ІйҖҗж—Ҙи®°еңЁж—Ҙзәҝ `$close` йҮҢ**пјҲе®һжөӢ 300280.SZ еі°еҖј 6.99вҶ’жңҖеҗҺжҲҗдәӨ 0.33 = вҲ’95%пјӣ000851.SZ 2.95вҶ’0.38 = вҲ’87%пјүпјҢжҢҒд»“жҜҸж—Ҙ MTM и·ҹзқҖи·ҢпјҢжңҖеҗҺеңЁеә•йғЁ force-close вҮ’ жҚҹеӨұе·Іе»әжЁЎпјҢ**еҶҚеҠ  haircut дјҡйҮҚеӨҚи®ЎжҚҹ** вҶ’ з”ЁжҲ·еҶіе®ҡпјҡдёҚеҠ  haircutпјҢж”№еҠ еӣәз¬¬ 4 еұӮеӣһйҖҖгҖӮдёӨеӨ„иҪҜиӮӢпјҡж—§йҖ»иҫ‘еҸӘзңӢ `prev_day` дёҖеӨ©пјҢеҸ–дёҚеҲ°зңҹе®һд»·ж—¶йҖҖеӣһ `avg_cost`пјҲеҒҸд№җи§ӮпјүпјҢдё”иӢҘжңҖеҗҺдёҖж №еңЁеҶҢ bar жҳҜ NaN еҒңзүҢиЎҢ вҶ’ `shares*NaN` вҶ’ зҺ°йҮ‘еҸҳ NaNгҖӮеҠ еӣәпјҡеј•ж“Һж–°еўһ `self._last_valid_price` **еҗ‘еүҚз»“иҪ¬зј“еӯҳ**пјҲеңЁ `_record_day` жҢүзңҹе®һ(йқһ NaNгҖҒ>0)ж”¶зӣҳйҖҗж—Ҙжӣҙж–°пјҢи·ЁеҒңзүҢзјәеҸЈдҝқз•ҷжңҖеҗҺзңҹе®һд»·пјү+ ж–° `_resolve_delist_price()` дјҳе…Ҳзә§ зҺ°йҮ‘жұЎжҹ“е…Ёз°ҝпјүгҖӮйҖҖеёӮж•°жҚ®жқҘжәҗе·ІзЎ®и®Өпјҡ`stock_basic.delist_date`пјҲTushare `list_status='L,D,P'`пјҢжҜҸиӮЎзІҫзЎ®йҖҖеёӮж—ҘпјҢ319 еҸӘжңүеҖјпјү+ `update_daily_data.py` жҜҸж—ҘйҮҚжҠ“иҰҶзӣ– вҶ’ жҒўеӨҚж•°жҚ®жӣҙж–°еҗҺиҮӘеҠЁдҝқйІңгҖӮжөӢиҜ•пјҡж–°еўһ [tests/backtest_engine/test_delisting_force_close.py](tests/backtest_engine/test_delisting_force_close.py)пјҲ13пјү+ `test_ranked_fallback_strategy.py` ж–°еўһ 2пјҲNaN з»“иҪ¬пјүпјӣдёӨеӨ„еқҮз»Ҹ"дёҙж—¶еӣһйҖҖиҜҒжҳҺжөӢиҜ•иғҪжҠ“ bug"йӘҢиҜҒпјӣ**backtest_engine е…ЁеҘ— 242 passed**гҖӮ`force_close ж°ёдёҚдә§з”ҹ NaN/иҙҹзҺ°йҮ‘` *Update Note (2026-06-08j, **ж•°жҚ®еӯ—ж®өдёҖиҮҙжҖ§е®Ўи®Ў + дҝ®еӨҚ A1/A2/A3пјҲз”ЁжҲ·жҢҮзӨәпјү**): еҜ№е…ЁйғЁ 35 дёӘжң¬ең° raw ж•°жҚ®йӣҶйҖҗеӯ—ж®өпјҲеӯҳеңЁжҖ§ + й»ҳи®ӨжҳҫзӨә + зұ»еһӢпјүз©·е°ҪжҜ”еҜ№ Tushare е®ҳж–№жҺҘеҸЈи§„иҢғпјҲзҰ»зәҝиҜӯж–ҷ `Tushareж•°жҚ®жҺҘеҸЈ/`пјүпјҢзЎ®е®ҡжҖ§йӣҶеҗҲ diffгҖӮз»“жһңпјҡ**PIT ж—Ҙжңҹй”ҡйӣ¶зјәеӨұгҖҒз”ҹдә§дё»ж•°жҚ®йӣҶеӯ—ж®өе®Ңж•ҙгҖҒж— ж•°еҖј-еӯҳжҲҗ-еӯ—з¬ҰдёІйҡҗжӮЈ**гҖӮе·Ҙе…· [audit_field_parity_vs_tushare.py](workspace/scripts/audit_field_parity_vs_tushare.py) вҶ’ [FINDINGS_AND_VERIFICATION.md](workspace/research/data_audit/FINDINGS_AND_VERIFICATION.md)пјҲ+ йҖҗж•°жҚ®йӣҶ diff + jsonпјүгҖӮ**дҝ®еӨҚ 3 йЎ№пјҲе®Ўи®ЎеӨҚи·‘йӘҢиҜҒйҖҡиҝҮпјү**пјҡ(A1) `stock_basic` зҡ„ fetch жјҸдәҶй»ҳи®Өеӯ—ж®ө `act_name`/`act_ent_type` вҶ’ иЎҘе…Ҙ fields йҮҚжҠ“пјҲ15вҶ’17 еҲ—пјҢ~99% йқһз©әпјҢж—§еӨҮд»Ҫпјүпјӣ(A3) `income_quarterly.ebit`/`ebitda` е®һжөӢ 0/459890 = 100% е…Ёз©әпјҲTushare еҚ•еӯЈ report_type 2/3 дёҚеЎ«зҙҜи®Ў-only еӯ—ж®өпјүвҶ’ еҲ еҲ—пјҲ72 ж–Үд»¶пјҢж—§еҪ’жЎЈпјү+ дёӨдёӘеҚ•еӯЈ fetcherпјҲincome/cashflow quarterlyпјүж”№ `dropna(how="all", axis=1)` йҳІеӨҚеҸ‘пјӣ(A2) жҢүз”ЁжҲ·жҢҮзӨә **`fina_indicator` еҸ–е…ЁйҮҸ 167 еӯ—ж®ө** вҖ”вҖ” `indicator_history_refresh.py` еҠ  `FINA_INDICATOR_ALL_FIELDS` еёёйҮҸгҖҒ`fetch_period` жҳҫејҸдј  `fields=`пјҢйҮҚи·‘ staged еҺҶеҸІ refreshпјҲ97 жңҹ / 550,537 иЎҢпјҢж—§еҪ’жЎЈ `_archive/indicators_pre_20260608_230015`пјүвҶ’ raw union **109вҶ’167 еҲ—**пјҢ58 дёӘзјәеӨұжҢҮж ҮеӣһеЎ«пјҲ`rd_exp`/`roe_avg`/`q_eps`/`q_roe`/`ebit_to_interest`/е‘ЁиҪ¬еӨ©ж•°/coverage жҜ”зҺҮвҖҰпјүгҖӮ**вҡ пёҸ A2 д»…е…Ҙ raw еұӮ**пјҡ58 ж–°еӯ—ж®өе°ҡжңӘиҝӣ PIT ledger / Qlib provider / `field_status.yaml`вҖ”вҖ”з ”з©¶/жӯЈејҸи·Ҝеҫ„иҰҒз”ЁйЎ» **ledger йҮҚе»ә вҶ’ provider йҮҚе»ә вҶ’ еӯ—ж®өжІ»зҗҶ**пјҲзӢ¬з«Ӣ gatedпјҢжңӘеҒҡпјүгҖӮsystemicпјҡеӨҡж•° fetcher дёҚдј  `fields=` еҸӘеҸ–й»ҳи®ӨеҲ—гҖӮи®°еҝҶ `project_field_parity_audit_2026_06_08`гҖӮ*

*Update Note (2026-06-08h, **report_rc PIT re-anchored to report_date+1 вҖ” validated PIT market-wide вҶ’ PR #41 MERGED; deep history 2010+ reclaimed**): the prior session called report_rc "forward-only" (PIT 2022-05+) because 100% of 2010-2021 rows carry `create_time=2022-05` (a Tushare bulk-backfill stamp). Tested directly against JoinQuant's genuine-PIT жңқйҳіж°ёз»ӯ дёҖиҮҙйў„жңҹ consensus (an INDEPENDENT vendor pipeline): `report_date+1` (=`strictly_next_open_trade_day`) reconstructs the PIT consensus вҖ” forecast-LEVEL Pearson/Spearman **+0.997** (5 stocksГ—4 dates vs `predicted_earnings_to_price_ratio`); forecast-ERROR parity reproduces the 2015/2017 cyclical regime sign-flips with the Tushare reconstruction *LESS* accurate than the oracle (= the OPPOSITE of lookahead; 15 stocksГ—7fy, 103 cells); and a BROAD survivorship-correct JQ cloud pull (3,712 stocks Г— 9 Jun-30 cross-sections 2013-2021) gives per-date Spearman mean **+0.940**, holding for the smallest size decile (+0.902) and later-delisted names (+0.932). So `create_time` is an INGESTION stamp, not proof `report_date` is unreliable. **Re-anchored `pit_backend.py build_ledger` report_rc branch:** trust create_time only when CONTEMPORANEOUS (calendar gap вүӨ `REPORT_RC_BACKFILL_GAP_DAYS=45`) вҶ’ `max(report_date,create_time)`; a bulk-backfill stamp (gap>45) or missing create_time вҶ’ `report_date + REPORT_RC_VENDOR_LAG_OPEN_DAYS(=2)` open days. 2023+ behavior byte-identical; backfilled deep history reclaimed (basket ledger eff-span moved 2022-05 вҶ’ **2010-01-07..2026-02-27**; `$report_rc__*` bins carry full-history events, иҢ…еҸ° 2005up/2297dn). **GPT 5.5 Pro post-impl review = MERGE-WITH-NITS**, all 4 nits applied+verified (gap on `.dt.normalize()`; build-time anchor-split audit log + clean-era canary [report_dateвүҘ2023 gap>45d вҶ’ WARN; real basket=0]; boundary test 45-trusted/46-ignored/-1-fallback; 2022-transition mixed-rows test). *Update Note (2026-06-08f, **RULE CHANGE вҖ” leverage is NOT a viable option in strategy research (user directive); doc-only**): per user instruction, added a non-negotiable research rule: research/evaluate/report every strategy **unlevered** (gross вүӨ 1Г— capital; no margin/borrowing past 100% invested), never propose leverage as a path to a return target, never headline a levered CAGR вҖ” the deployable number is the 1Г— number; long-only = fully-invested-or-cash, market-neutral = natural 1Г— (funded long/short). Rationale: leverage adds no edge, only multiplies vol+drawdown, and is self-defeating on a high-vol long-only book; deployment context assumes no leverage. Added to **CLAUDE.md В§7 item 11**, **AGENTS.md В§2a.3**, and **`.agents/rules/research-integrity.md` В§8b** (mirrored same pass per В§11.2). `config.yaml risk.max_leverage=1.5` left as a legacy field but flagged in the rule as NOT license to lever (not edited). NOTE this supersedes the leverage-frontier framing in the 2026-06-08 low-corr/MN research (`jq_replication/FINDINGS_lowcorr.md` + [[research_long_only_50cagr]]): the levered "~5Г— MN вҶ’ ~50% CAGR" and "leveraged long-only" paths are now OUT OF SCOPE вҖ” the honest deployable ceiling is the 1Г— figure (long-only VQ10 ~+20.7%/вҲ’26.6%; unlevered low-corr MN Sharpe ~1.4-1.8 / CAGR ~12-15%). 50% CAGR is therefore NOT attainable in-scope.*

*Update Note (2026-06-04, **New hard invariant вҖ” price-return (vectorized) vs total-return (event-driven) added to `CLAUDE.md` В§3.3 + В§8.2 / `AGENTS.md` В§2a.3; doc-only**): promoted the long_only finding (note further below) into a standing backtest-fidelity invariant after verifying the mechanism in code, not from the summary. `VectorizedBacktester` defaults to `deal_price='close'` and computes returns from the provider's RAW `$close` вҶ’ PRICE return (a dividend/bonus ex-date drops price without crediting the distribution). `EventDrivenBacktester` credits post-tax cash dividends + bonus shares on the ex-date via [corporate_actions.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/corporate_actions.py) `CorporateActionHandler.process` (`cash_div_tax * shares` вҶ’ `portfolio.credit_cash`; `stk_div * shares` вҶ’ position) вҶ’ TOTAL return. They diverge by ~the book's dividend yield: long_only value book EventDriven +11.64% vs vectorized +6.17% CAGR (2021-26); the phase6d monkeypatch that no-op'd `CorporateActionHandler.process` collapsed EventDriven to +6.59% вүҲ vectorized = the isolating proof (dividends+bonus = +5.05% CAGR; not a leak/bug). Rule: never compare a vectorized price-return screen against an event-driven total-return run for a dividend-paying strategy without accounting for the gap; the event-driven total-return figure is the deployment number. Empirical finding, NO unit-test gate yet вҖ” candidate follow-up: a dividend-fixture regression pinning the `CorporateActionHandler.process` crediting + a vectorized-price-return-vs-event-total-return assertion. Doc-only; mirrored CLAUDEвҶ”AGENTS in the same pass per В§11.2.*

*Update Note (2026-06-02, **EventDrivenBacktester limit detection switched to Tushare stk_limit (primary) with computed-band fallback; stk_limit promoted quarantineвҶ’approved**): the event-driven engine previously ALWAYS recomputed limit-up/limit-down prices from `pre_close Г— regulatory band`. It now resolves through the new `Exchange.resolve_limit_prices()` ([src/backtest_engine/event_driven/exchange.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/exchange.py)), which **prefers Tushare's published `$up_limit` / `$down_limit`** (the exchange's own daily limit prices, already materialized as bare-name day bins) and **falls back to the computed round-half-up band** only when those fields are absent/NaN. `is_limit_up` / `is_limit_down` now detect against the resolved prices (so `strategies.RankedFallbackStrategy` and `can_buy` / `can_sell` inherit it). `$up_limit` / `$down_limit` were added to `ENGINE_REQUIRED_FIELDS` ([constants.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/constants.py)) so formal runs preload them and never fall into per-day `D.features`; `_fetch_day_data` now derives its fetch list from `ENGINE_REQUIRED_FIELDS` (single source of truth) and renames the two columns. **Why Tushare-primary:** the published values carry the exact fen-rounding, the ex-rights adjustment, and special regimes the band formula misses (the pre-2023 main-board IPO-first-day +44%/вҲ’36% asymmetric rule; and post-2023 registration-system IPO no-limit windows encoded as a wide sentinel up_limitвүҲ1e6 / down_limitвүҲ0.01). **Why a fallback is still needed (empirically verified, not assumed):** [workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_coverage.py](workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_coverage.py) scanned traded stock-days (vol>0, real stocks only, indices excluded) across 2014/2018/2021/2024/2026 вҖ” **2024+ has zero holes**, but pre-2022 has small explained holes (2021 = 2.17%, dominated by Beijing-Stock-Exchange names during the 2021 launch where Tushare had no `stk_limit` row yet; plus IPO no-limit days and a few legacy main-board names). Value sanity: вүҘ99.79% of present rows land on a regulatory tier (Вұ5/10/20/30%) (worst window 2021 = 99.7957%; 2024/2026 вүҲ 99.94/99.96%); the residual is no-limit sentinel rows (registration-system IPO no-limit days, counted off-tier because their implied band is ~thousands of %), the pre-2023 main-board IPO first-day +44%/вҲ’36% rule, and penny-stock fen-rounding вҖ” all correct. **Governance (user-approved full promotion):** `stk_limit` moved `quarantine вҶ’ approved` in [config/field_registry/field_status.yaml](config/field_registry/field_status.yaml) with a bound approval YAML ([config/field_registry/approvals/2026-06-02_stk_limit_quarantine_to_approved.yaml](config/field_registry/approvals/2026-06-02_stk_limit_quarantine_to_approved.yaml), bound to `provider_build_id=prod_full_20260421_namespace_v1` / `calendar_policy_id=frozen_20260227_system_build`) + an append-only [field_approval_log.jsonl](config/field_registry/field_approval_log.jsonl) entry. These are execution fields knowable at session open (pre-determined from the prior close), so no `Ref` lag is required. **Tests:** new `tests/backtest_engine/test_exchange_limits.py::ResolveLimitPricesTests` (primary-beats-computed, IPO-44% case, fallback-on-absent/NaN); `tests/data_infra/test_field_registry.py::TestLiveRegistry::test_stk_limit_bare_fields_approved_for_formal` (flipped from the old quarantine assertion). Sweep: 68 (exchange-limits + field-registry) + 125 (preload-hardening + approval-evidence + field-dependency-gate + PR9 compat) + 11 (event-driven wiring + dormant-module boundaries) all green; both lints (`no_bare_qlib_features`, `unsafe_pit_dates`) clean; end-to-end smoke confirms the fields preload and the exchange detects limits via them. Docs synced: CLAUDE.md В§3 (new invariant + PR5 seed line + PR9a guardrail line), AGENTS.md (mirror), [src/backtest_engine/README.md](src/backtest_engine/README.md), [data/data_dictionary.md](data/data_dictionary.md). No on-disk / pipeline change вҖ” the bins already existed; the engine now consumes what it had materialized. **Verified no-limit-day behavior:** Tushare encodes genuinely-no-limit stock-days (ChiNext/STAR/post-2023 main-board first 5 days; BSE listing day) as a WIDE SENTINEL (`up_limitвүҲ1e5/1e6`, `down_limitвүҲ0.01/0.00`), NOT NaN вҖ” so the primary path correctly treats them as freely tradable (close never within 0.005 of the sentinel); true non-stock instruments (indices) are the only NaN rows. Evidence: [workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_nolimit_days.py](workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_nolimit_days.py); pinned by `test_no_limit_day_sentinel_is_not_a_limit` / `test_no_limit_day_bse_sentinel`. **KNOWN FOLLOW-UP (deferred to a future task, chip spawned 2026-06-02):** in OLDER provider data (pre-~2022; e.g. the ~6952 IPO-window NaN rows seen in 2018) some no-limit IPO days were published as NaN rather than the sentinel, so they hit the computed-band fallback; `can_buy` is protected by `is_ipo_period()` but `can_sell` has no IPO override, so a no-limit IPO day that closes exactly on the spurious computed `limit_down` could be wrongly blocked from selling. Rare, pre-2022 only, NOT a regression (the prior computed-only code behaved identically). Candidate fix: add an `is_ipo_period()` short-circuit to `can_sell` (symmetric with `can_buy`) and/or have `resolve_limit_prices` return a no-limit sentinel when `is_ipo_period()` is True, with a regression test in [tests/backtest_engine/test_exchange_limits.py](tests/backtest_engine/test_exchange_limits.py).*

*Update Note (2026-06-01, **Factor-lifecycle formalization PHASE 6 COMPLETE вҖ” first operational `factor_lifecycle` run; 72 base factors promoted draftвҶ’candidate on the LIVE registry** (branch `factor-lifecycle-p6`)): ran the Phase-5 IS-only gate on the **147 base catalog factors** end-to-end through the orchestrator. **Result: 72 promoted to `status=candidate`** (+ 72 definition-bound FORMAL evidence rows, `formal_evidence_eligible=True`, `oos_rank_icir`=NA [no OOS leak], NEVER `approved`); live registry now **72 candidate + 99 draft** (171 current). **Pipeline:** 147 base вҶ’ 114 field-eligible (33 quarantine/pending `$field` auto-excluded: alpha_*/flow_*/margin_*/north_*) вҶ’ 85 IS-candidates (|heldout rank_icir|вүҘ0.10 вҲ§ yearly sign-consistencyвүҘ0.70) вҶ’ **72 promoted = the OOS-stable subset** (the 13 IS-candidates whose INDEPENDENT full-window 2014-2026 evidence collapses/flips OOS were EXCLUDED from the consumed batch; 8 of those 13 are the `grow_*`/`earn_earnings_momentum` earnings-LEVEL factors already known IS-overfit). User chose "promote 72 OOS-stable only" (vs all 85) after the clarification that **`candidate` is an ADDITIVE tier вҖ” it does NOT restrict research use** (`get_factor_catalog()` stays authoritative for ALL discovery/sandbox; the registry status gates only FORMAL hypothesis_validation components, and `candidate` can never auto-become `approved` вҖ” that needs the separate P1.1 OOS/promotion gate). **GPT-mandated safety arc honored:** compute-only dry-run ([phase6_factor_lifecycle_dry_run.py](workspace/scripts/phase6_factor_lifecycle_dry_run.py), cross-checked vs the prior catalog-revalidation CSV вҖ” IS ICIR reproduces) вҶ’ temp-registry orchestrator validation (3-factor end-to-end) вҶ’ live sync вҶ’ live 72-run. **TWO real merged-code bugs found by the operational run + fixed (each with a regression test proven to fail pre-fix):** (1) **Phase-4 MultiIndex level-order** вҖ” [build_is_windowed_panel](src/alpha_research/factor_lifecycle/walk_forward_validation.py) hardcoded an `(instrument,datetime)` future-price index, but `compute_factors` returns `(datetime,instrument)`; the POSITIONAL `adj.reindex` matched NOTHING вҶ’ all-NaN label вҶ’ empty-panel `IsEndLeakageError`. The Phase-4 fixtures only ever used `(instrument,datetime)` so the integration point was untested. Fixed: build the future index in the panel's actual level order (robust to either) + a loud guard if current prices match but all future prices are NaN. Regression: `test_build_is_multiindex_level_order_invariant`. (2) **Phase-5 publish resume-safety** вҖ” [factor_lifecycle_registry_publish](src/research_orchestrator/factor_lifecycle_steps.py) read verdicts from the in-memory `context.state["factor_lifecycle"]`, but the gate pauses split the run across processes and `reconstruct_state_from_completed_steps` restores ONLY `step_outputs` on resume вҶ’ on a real (paused) run it would promote NOTHING. Fixed: read verdicts from the PERSISTED `factor_lifecycle_walk_forward` step_outputs (in-memory fallback for the no-pause path). Regression: `test_publish_reads_verdicts_from_persisted_step_outputs_on_resume`. **1-factor benign sync:** `rev_up_down_ratio_20d` re-versioned to v3 (catalog refactored `Count(вҖҰ>0,20)/20`вҶ’equivalent `Sum(If(вҖҰ>0,1,0),20)/20`; same factor, drifted hash) via `sync_catalog_to_registry` so the resolver P1.3 gate passed (it's in the 72). **Run mechanics for reuse:** factor_lifecycle is formal-only вҶ’ needs a Hypothesis (no floor rails apply вҖ” not in `SUCCESS_CRITERIA_FLOORS`); success_criteria sets ONLY `min_rank_icir` (others None вҶ’ no null hard rules вҶ’ automated verdict honestly "accepted"); the 2 gate pauses are driven by [phase6_drive_gates.py](workspace/scripts/phase6_drive_gates.py) (concern scores keyed to `min_rank_icir`, then `gate_decision=approved`); request built by [phase6_setup_request.py](workspace/scripts/phase6_setup_request.py). Tests: factor_lifecycle+registry suite 81 passed. **NOT done / follow-ups:** the **24 composite + industry-relative** factors (Layer-2 `add_composites` gating); the **6 sealed-OOS expansion winners** still take their SEPARATE governed sealed-OOS / promotion path (register definitions first); the user's OOS-fix **WIP is still STASHED** at `stash@{0}` (restore via `git stash pop` вҖ” disjoint from this work). **Committed `38ba203` on `factor-lifecycle-p6`; PR [#35](https://github.com/henrydan111/quant-system/pull/35) вҶ’ `wave1-field-promotion`.** **GPT PR-#35 cross-review = GO to merge** (both fixes confirmed correct + complete, no code-level leakage hole, 57 focused tests pass, live-registry probe matches: 72 candidate / 99 draft / 0 approved, 72 definition-bound formal_evidence_eligible rows, no non-null OOS metric) **with one governance follow-up (resolved, not a merge blocker):** the 72 are an **`oos_informed_backfill`** вҖ” the IS-only validator was NOT contaminated (OOS never entered labels/folds/metrics/set_status; evidence rows are IS-only), but the SELECTION of which factors became candidate used pre-existing full-window OOS knowledge to exclude the 13 collapsers, so **the 72 must NEVER be described later as a fresh OOS-free selection**, and **2021-2026 is ALREADY BURNED for these 72** (a future candidateвҶ’approved promotion MUST use a genuinely-sealed window, not 2021-2026). *Update Note (2026-05-30, **Clean-PIT long-only strategy research вҖ” 50%-CAGR target shown INFEASIBLE; honest defensive deliverable**): Autonomous research effort (workspace/research/long_only_50cagr/) to build a PIT-safe, non-overfit long-only A-share strategy at 50%+ CAGR / <30% MDD. ALL factors via `compute_factors()`вҶ’`qlib_windowed_features` (sanctioned PIT-safe wrapper, Ref-shifted); IS=2014-2020, sealed OOS=2021-01вҶ’2026-02 (run ONCE, stage='oos_test'). **Findings:** (1) A-shares are a reversal/low-risk/liquidity-premium market вҖ” short/medium "momentum" has NEGATIVE IC; (2) **cross-sectional IC does NOT convert to long-only top-K return** вҖ” reversal (ICIR вҲ’0.44) AND a walk-forward LightGBM (test RankIC +0.05-0.07) both produce catastrophic long-only top-K (вҲ’8.7%/вҲ’78% MDD; ML вҲ’21%/вҲ’49% in 2018) because top-decile = high-beta falling-knives; (3) only VALUE + LOW-VOLATILITY work long-only (defensive low-beta names survive concentration); (4) small/microcap tilt HURTS even with overlay; (5) CSI300-MA120 trend Г— vol-targeting overlay lifts IS Sharpe to ~1.24 and IS MDD<30% but **did NOT generalize OOS (whipsawed, +6.2%вҶ’+0.7%)**. **Sealed OOS champion (VL value+lowrisk @ core-liquid, equal-wt top-40, monthly, RAW no-overlay): +6.17% CAGR, вҲ’19.0% MDD, Sharpe 0.47 вҖ” vs all benchmarks вҲ’42% to вҲ’46% MDD; +25% in the 2024 microcap crash (flight to quality).** **50%/<30% is INFEASIBLE on clean PIT long-only** (requires sustained Sharpe ~3.8; best clean OOS Sharpe found = 0.47) вҖ” reconfirms the invalidated val_heavy/11F "190% champions" were lookahead. Deployable = the defensive value+low-vol top-40 (NOT the overlay). Recommended next: EventDrivenBacktester tradability check before any promotion (promotion gate per В§3 requires independent PIT-correct reproduction). Full writeup: workspace/research/long_only_50cagr/FINDINGS.md. NOTE: this is research only вҖ” no registry/master-table writes, no rule changes.*

*Update Note (2026-05-29, **PIT LOOKAHEAD BUG in the sandbox factor loaders вҖ” INVALIDATES all v31/v32/v33 + val_heavy sandbox performance numbers, including the two 2026-05-29 notes below**): A string-comparison lookahead bug was found in `build_pit_pivot()` across the entire `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v*` family (58 scripts). **Root cause**: `effective_date` (stored datetime64 in `data/pit_ledger/indicators/indicators.parquet`) was cast with `.astype(str)` вҶ’ dashed ISO `"2018-10-30"`, then lexically merged/ffilled against COMPACT `trade_date` `"20180607"`. Since ASCII `-`(0x2D) < `0`(0x30), every dashed `Y-MM-DD` sorts BELOW even January-Y's compact trade dates, so the ffill served the calendar year's LAST-published quarter (вүҲQ3, effective late-Oct) from January onward вҖ” up to ~9 months of earnings foresight on every fundamental factor AND the eligibility filter. Confirmed on disk (600519: June-2018 served Q3 `roa 25.25` instead of the correct Q1 `9.05`). **SCOPE VERDICT вҖ” the bug is CONFINED to the sandbox hand-rolled loaders; the production backend is CLEAN**: `src/data_infra/pit_backend.py` normalizes all dates via `normalize_date_series()`вҶ’datetime64 and aligns with `calendar.searchsorted()` on a `DatetimeIndex` (Timestamp comparisons, never strings); the only date-`sorted(set|set)` in `src/` (`pit_backend.py:1256`) operates on already-normalized Timestamps. Verified empirically: the live Qlib provider serves `$roa` for 600519 stepping EXACTLY on each report's `effective_date` (June=Q1=9.05, not Q3). `EventDrivenBacktester` / `VectorizedBacktester` / research orchestrator all read via `D.features()` (datetime calendar) and are unaffected. The JQ deployment script (`workspace/scripts/jq_11f_roewaa_strategy.py`) uses JoinQuant-native `get_fundamentals(date=)` + `pubDate` filtering and is ALSO PIT-correct (no bug). **FIX**: all 58 sandbox loaders patched вҖ” `effective_date` normalized to compact `%Y%m%d` (`pd.to_datetime(...).dt.strftime`) + a permanent `assert ...str.fullmatch(r"\d{8}")` PIT-leak guard; proven full-series identical to a datetime-correct reference. **RE-MEASUREMENT (same sandbox engine, loader the ONLY variable changed)**: (a) **v33 champion 11F+roe_waa** вҖ” OOS CAGR 188.7%вҶ’**2.0%**, MDD -33.8%вҶ’**-76.3%**, WF ~213%вҶ’**16.9%**; FAILS all gates. (b) **val_heavy deployed config** (K6_min70 вҖ” the +81.9%/MDD-29.2%/WF+82.4% "FINAL deployment" recorded in prior memory) вҖ” CAGRвҶ’**+9.6%**, MDDвҶ’**-65.1%**, WFвҶ’**-3.4% (negative)**; 0/18 param configs and 0/9 rebal configs pass. The lookahead contributed вүҲ71pp of CAGR and вүҲ85pp of walk-forward. **CONSEQUENCE вҖ” the v31/v32/v33 + val_heavy edge was almost entirely earnings foresight, NOT tradable alpha.** The two 2026-05-29 notes below (v33 EventDrivenBacktester 77.8% OOS / 106.4% full; v32 open-execution 190.8% OOS) and the v31/v33 specs are INVALIDATED вҖ” every one of those numbers consumed the contaminated sandbox factor arrays (v33 imports `v32.load_data`; post-fix v32 IS=55% but OOS=2%). The live JQ script will not LEAK (it is PIT-safe) but also will NOT deliver the performance it was selected on; its true expected profile fails every gate. **Any live or pending deployment of the val_heavy / 11F-roe_waa strategy should be halted pending a clean, from-scratch re-derivation on PIT-correct factors (preferably through the production backend / EventDrivenBacktester, not a hand-rolled sandbox loader).** Bug report: `workspace/research/jq_deployment/v33_PIT_lookahead_bug_report.md`. Re-measurement logs: `workspace/outputs/v32_rerun_fixed.log`, `workspace/outputs/v15o_rerun_fixed.log`.*

*Update Note (2026-05-28, PR 10c вҖ” Approval-evidence explicit-exemption contract; **closes GPT 5.5 Pro round-7 review of PR 10b**): GPT 5.5 Pro's round-7 review confirmed the PR 10b null/blank fix landed correctly but flagged the last fail-open path: an approval YAML missing BOTH `provider_build_id` and `calendar_policy_id` was still silently skipped as "legacy", which could not distinguish a true non-provider-bound record from a new approval that ACCIDENTALLY omitted both keys. The approvals README template also still omitted the binding keys, so a future approval written from it would inherit the silent skip. PR 10c closes both on the same `pr10-followups-after-pr9-merge` branch BEFORE PR #15 merges. **Fix**: `load_approval_bindings` ([src/data_infra/approval_evidence.py](src/data_infra/approval_evidence.py)) now requires an unbound record to declare `binding_exempt: true` (strict bool вҖ” a string `"true"` or `binding_exempt: false` does NOT exempt) with a non-empty `binding_exempt_reason`; both-absent WITHOUT a valid exemption raises `ApprovalEvidenceConfigError`. A contradiction guard raises when both binding keys are present AND `binding_exempt: true` (a provider-bound approval cannot be exempt). New full contract: (a) both keys present non-empty strings вҶ’ validated; (b) exactly one key вҶ’ raise; (c) either value null/blank/non-string вҶ’ raise; (d) both absent + valid `binding_exempt` вҶ’ skip; (e) both absent without exemption вҶ’ raise; (f) both present + `binding_exempt: true` вҶ’ raise. **Committed-YAML + README updates**: [2026-05-27_quarantine_prefix_fix.yaml](config/field_registry/approvals/2026-05-27_quarantine_prefix_fix.yaml) (a coverage/diagnostic fix that promotes nothing to formal use) gains `binding_exempt: true` + reason вҖ” it was previously skipped via the both-absent silent path. [approvals/README.md](config/field_registry/approvals/README.md) required-fields template now includes `provider_build_id` + `calendar_policy_id` and a dedicated section documents the `binding_exempt` escape hatch for non-provider-bound administrative records. The indicators approval YAML already carries a real binding (validated, unchanged). **Tests**: PR 10c brings the approval-evidence test count from 29 to 39 вҖ” new `TestBindingExemptContract` (7: both-absent-no-exemption raises, exempt-without-reason raises, exempt-blank-reason raises, exempt+reason skipped, `binding_exempt: false` raises, string-`"true"` raises, both-bound+exempt contradiction raises), new `TestCommittedApprovalsSatisfyContract` (2: live committed approvals dir loads without raising + indicators binding present; quarantine_prefix_fix is exempt-skipped not bound), plus flips the two pre-PR-10c both-absent-skip tests to expect a raise and adds an explicit-exemption skip test. **Regression**: full sweep `pytest tests/research_orchestrator/ tests/data_infra/ tests/backtest_engine/ tests/architecture/ tests/alpha_research/test_factor_library_pit_safety.py -q` returns **564 pass, 9 skip** in ~14s (+10 vs PR 10b baseline 554). `scripts/lint_no_bare_qlib_features.py src/` clean. **CLAUDE.md updated**: PR 10's entry header now reads "hardened by PR 10a + PR 10b + PR 10c"; 1 new dedicated PR 10c entry. **Governance arc status**: the approval-evidence scanner now fails closed on malformed, non-mapping, partial, null/blank/non-string, both-absent-unmarked, and contradictory YAMLs вҖ” every fail-open path GPT 5.5 Pro surfaced across rounds 6вҖ“7 is closed. **Branch**: same as PR 10/10a/10b; PR 10c lands as a follow-up commit to update PR #15.*

*Update Note (2026-05-29, v33 вҖ” CHAMPION RUN THROUGH EventDrivenBacktester: sandbox 190.8% OOS collapses to 77.8% under realistic execution, AND reveals a deployment ceiling): The v31/v32 sandbox uses a custom vectorized NAV loop that ignores T+1, limit-up unfillability, suspension, board lots, real cost breakdowns, and slippage. v33 (`workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15aa_v33_event_driven.py`) keeps the SIGNAL byte-identical to v32 (imports the v32 module, calls load_data(), reuses its exact universe filter + F11_ROEWAA scoring to build an oversampled top-15 ranked schedule + per-rebalance vol-scale) but routes EXECUTION through `src/backtest_engine/event_driven` via a `ConcentratedRankedStrategy(RankedFallbackStrategy)` (JoinQuant filter_limitup substitution + top-2/next-3 concentration + vol scaling). Run: full 2014-01-02вҶ’2026-02-27, CNY 1,000,000, bench 000300.SH, fill=open_close, CostConfig() JQ-default + JOINQUANT_DEFAULT_SLIPPAGE, T+1/multi-tier limits/ST guard/board lots ON, suspension via vol==0 fallback (ranges parquet absent), volume_limit=0.25, sandbox mode (run_mode=None вҖ” execution realism without formal governance gates). **RESULTS (full period)**: CAGR=106.4%, MDD=-28.94%, Sharpe=2.57, win-rate 71.6%, P/L 2.44, 1374 trades, 58 BLOCKED orders. **IS(14-19)=140.1%, OOS(20-26)=77.8%, OOS MDD=-19.44%.** **THREE-WAY (OOS 2020-2026)**: v32 sandbox 190.8% / -34.84% вҶ’ v33 event-driven 77.8% / -19.44% вҶ’ JoinQuant live ~7.77% / -45.82%. **DECISIVE FINDING вҖ” the strategy has a real tradability/deployment ceiling the sandbox completely hid**: OOS deployment averaged only **59.3%** (vs the ~95.4% vol-scale target), i.e. ~40% of capital sat in cash because the signal selects high-momentum quality names that systematically lock limit-up and cannot be bought (IS deployment was 92.3% вҖ” the unbuyability is far worse in the 2020-2026 momentum regime). n_positions OOS mean=7.08 (mode 6, tail to 13) vs target 5 вҖ” stuck/un-sellable positions accumulate under T+1 + suspension/limit-down. The low -19.44% OOS MDD is therefore largely a **cash-drag artifact, NOT genuine risk control**. **GAP DECOMPOSITION**: (a) sandboxвҶ’v33 (190.8%вҶ’77.8%, -113pp) = execution friction + the deployment ceiling (can't put 40% of capital to work); (b) v33вҶ’JQ-live (77.8%вҶ’7.77%, -70pp) is NOT execution (v33 already models it) вҖ” it is SIGNAL-CONSTRUCTION difference: the JQ script used JQ `indicator.*` fields with the parent-company-equity bug + single-quarter reconstruction + excluded з§‘еҲӣ/еҢ—дәӨ/ж¬Ўж–°(375d), whereas v33 uses the clean pre-computed Tushare q_roe/q_dt_roe/q_op_qoq fields over the full universe. **The multiple-comparison caveat from the v31 audit still applies to 77.8%** (signal iterated ~20x against OOS v17вҶ’v32; bias-corrected lower). **HONEST BOTTOM LINE**: on the clean signal with realistic execution the strategy is materially weaker than the 190% sandbox headline AND capacity-constrained (can't deploy >~60% in momentum regimes); it is NOT the 190% strategy. Outputs: `workspace/outputs/v33_event_driven_results.txt`, `v33_event_driven_report.parquet`. Minor: v33 added a 2-line additive `COL_ORDER` global to v32 (exposes ts_code-per-array-column for the harness; no behavior change to v32 results).*

*Update Note (2026-05-28, PR 10b вҖ” Approval-evidence null/blank-value fail-closed; **closes GPT 5.5 Pro round-7 review of PR 10a**): GPT 5.5 Pro's round-7 review of PR #15 confirmed all 3 PR 10a fixes landed correctly, but found one remaining fail-open edge case in the governance scanner: an approval YAML that KEEPS the `provider_build_id` / `calendar_policy_id` keys but blanks their VALUES (e.g. `provider_build_id:` with no value, during a manual provider rebuild) was silently skipped as legacy. Root cause: `load_approval_bindings` used `data.get("provider_build_id")`, which returns `None` for BOTH an absent key AND a key present with a null value. PR 10b closes it on the same `pr10-followups-after-pr9-merge` branch BEFORE PR #15 merges. **Fix**: `load_approval_bindings` now uses `"provider_build_id" in data` for key PRESENCE (decoupled from value), then requires each present value to be a non-empty string after `.strip()`. New contract: (a) both keys absent вҶ’ legacy skip; (b) exactly one key present вҶ’ `ApprovalEvidenceConfigError`; (c) both present but EITHER value null / `""` / whitespace / non-string вҶ’ `ApprovalEvidenceConfigError`; (d) both present non-empty strings вҶ’ validated, values stored stripped (so a trailing-space binding still matches a clean manifest value). The module docstring's "SHOULD carry both keys" wording is upgraded to the stricter "MUST carry both keys with non-empty string values" contract. **Tests**: PR 10b adds `TestNullOrBlankBindingFailsClosed` (8 tests): both-null raises, both-empty-string raises, both-whitespace raises, one-null-one-absent raises, one-valid-one-null raises, non-string value raises, true-legacy-neither-key still skipped, valid-nonempty-strings pass + stored stripped + match clean manifest. *Update Note (2026-05-29, v32 вҖ” EXECUTION-MODEL CORRECTION: close[T-1] вҶ’ open[T]; champion moves fp=0.66 вҶ’ fp=0.65): The v31 PIT audit (this session) confirmed v31 is fully PIT-safe (all 11 factors use `effective_date`+`shift(1)`; 304,546/304,546 indicator rows verified `effective_date > ann_date` strictly) and the CAGR formula is mathematically correct, BUT flagged one optimistic execution assumption: v31's `sim()` builds the basket at index `i` from PIT-shifted (T-1) factors вҖ” correct вҖ” then applies `ret_arr[i]=pct_chg[T]=close[T-1]вҶ’close[T]` as the rebalance-day return, implicitly assuming you can BUY at close[T-1] and capture the overnight gap for free. **v32** (`workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15aa_v32_open_execution.py`) fixes this with realistic open[T] execution: decision still at close[T-1], but on rebalance day the OLD basket earns only the overnight gap `open[T]/pre_close[T]-1` before being sold at the open, and the NEW basket earns `close[T]/open[T]-1` (openвҶ’close). Identity `(1+gap)В·(1+o2c)==1+pct_chg` verified on disk (max|err|=6.5e-4, corporate-action edge cells only). Everything else IDENTICAL to v31 (same factors, weights, K=5, REBAL=15, vol scaling, flat 50bps cost, NaN handling, CAGR/MDD/WF/JK formulas). **KEY FINDING вҖ” the execution drag is SMALL on OOS but concentrated in the 2014-2015 bubble**: OOS (2020-2026) delta is only **-0.6pp** across all focus_pct (11F fp0.63: OOS 188.7%вҶ’188.1%); but IS (2014-2019) delta is **-18.9pp** (275.8%вҶ’256.9%) and full-period CAGR delta ~-8pp. Reason: A-share overnight gaps were enormous during the 2014-2015 limit-up bubble (close-execution captured huge free overnight moves there) but are near-zero in the modern 2020+ regime (mean overnight gap across all cells = +0.0073%). So the deployable OOS estimate is barely affected, but the headline full-period/IS numbers were inflated by a 2014-2015 artifact. **CHAMPION CHANGE**: under open-execution, MDD worsens ~0.4-1.2pp across the board (giving up overnight gaps lowers NAV peaks): fp=0.63 MDD -33.84%вҶ’-34.23%, fp=0.65 -33.91%вҶ’-34.84%, fp=0.66 -33.95%вҶ’**-35.15% (FAILS -35% gate)**. New deployable champion = **11F+roe_waa @ fp=0.65: OOS=190.8%, JK_min=206.8%, MDD=-34.84%, WF=200.3%, all PASS**. fp=0.66 is now rejected. v32 also re-confirmed 10F baseline (OOS 184.0%вҶ’183.2%, -0.8pp). JK_min deltas -8.9 to -9.3pp (full-period JK reflects the IS-period bubble drag). Output: `workspace/outputs/v32_results.txt`. **The v32 OOS numbers remain subject to the multiple-comparison caveat from the audit (192.7%/190.8% headlines were iterated against the OOS window across ~20 versions v17вҶ’v32; bias-corrected clean-OOS expectation ~120-150%).** Next: the JoinQuant live deployment must use open[T] execution (it already does вҖ” `run_daily(time='09:30')` fills at open), so the v32 numbers are the correct sim-side comparison for JQ.*

*Update Note (2026-05-28, PR 10a вҖ” Approval-evidence fail-closed hardening; **closes GPT 5.5 Pro round-6 review of PR 10**): GPT 5.5 Pro's round-6 review of PR #15 accepted the AGENTS.md sync and catalog count refresh, accepted the approval-evidence direction, but found 3 fail-open paths in the original implementation. PR 10a closes all 3 on the same `pr10-followups-after-pr9-merge` branch BEFORE PR #15 merges. **Blockers fixed**: (1) **Hardcoded manifest path** вҖ” pre-PR-10a `_approval_evidence_binding_check` hardcoded `data/qlib_data/metadata/provider_build.json` while `_provider_manifest_check` resolved from `config.yaml::storage.qlib_data_dir`. The mismatch meant a non-default provider host could see the provider check validate one tree and the approval-evidence check validate a different (or missing) one. PR 10a factors out `_resolve_qlib_dir_from_config(project_root=None)` and uses it from both audit blocks. Critical detail: the helper uses a `project_root=None` sentinel (NOT `PROJECT_ROOT` as a default arg) because Python evaluates default args at function-definition time, which would have frozen the original value and broken the PR 8d behavioral test that monkey-patches `run_daily_qa.PROJECT_ROOT` at runtime. (2) **Partial bindings as wildcard match** вҖ” pre-PR-10a, an approval YAML with only `provider_build_id` (no `calendar_policy_id`, or vice-versa) was silently treated as wildcard match on the missing axis, reducing the binding from two dimensions to one. PR 10a's `load_approval_bindings` raises `ApprovalEvidenceConfigError` when exactly one binding key is declared. New contract: both absent = legacy skip; both present = validated; exactly one = hard fail with diagnostic naming the missing key. (3) **Malformed / non-dict YAMLs silently skipped** вҖ” pre-PR-10a, YAML parse errors and non-mapping top levels were logged-and-skipped, a fail-open path that could silently disappear a governance YAML. PR 10a converts both to `ApprovalEvidenceConfigError`. Empty YAMLs (parse to `None`) also raise. The post-PR-10a `evaluate_approval_evidence_bindings` removes the wildcard-match logic entirely because `load_approval_bindings` now guarantees both axes are non-None for every returned binding. **Tests**: PR 10a brings the approval-evidence test count from 13 to 21 вҖ” 3 partial-binding tests (provider-only raises, calendar-only raises, error propagates through eval), 3 malformed-YAML tests (parse failure raises, non-dict raises, empty YAML raises), 1 new daily-QA source-level test proving both audit blocks use the shared `_resolve_qlib_dir_from_config` helper AND that the hardcoded `PROJECT_ROOT / "data" / "qlib_data"` is gone, plus 2 behavioral tests (`test_approval_evidence_check_uses_configured_qlib_dir` and `test_approval_evidence_check_surfaces_drift_against_configured_dir`) that set up a temp project root with a custom `config.yaml::storage.qlib_data_dir` and verify the check (a) finds the manifest at the configured location, (b) reports `ok=True` on matched binding, (c) reports `ok=False` on drift with diagnostic naming both declared (old) and current (new) build_ids. **Regression**: full sweep returns **546 pass, 9 skip** in ~14s (+8 vs PR 10 baseline 538). The PR 8d behavioral test `test_mismatched_calendar_returns_not_ok` regressed temporarily on the first PR 10a iteration due to the default-arg-at-def-time bug; the `project_root=None` sentinel fix restores it. `scripts/lint_no_bare_qlib_features.py src/` clean. **CLAUDE.md updated**: PR 10's hard-invariant entry expanded to reference the PR 10a hardening + 1 new entry. **Non-blocking deferral** (GPT round-6 explicit): release-gate wiring of `approval_evidence` is NOT in PR 10a вҖ” daily QA is the operational health gate today; a future PR can add the release-gate hook as a stronger defense-in-depth for publication paths. **Branch**: same as PR 10; PR 10a lands as a follow-up commit to update PR #15.*

*Update Note (2026-05-28, PR 9b вҖ” Universe raw-field gate at resolver + dataset_build defense-in-depth; **closes GPT 5.5 Pro round-4 review of PR 9a**): GPT 5.5 Pro's round-4 review of PR #14 (PR 9 + PR 9a) accepted all PR 9a fixes and identified one remaining merge blocker: the field gate in `handle_validation_object_resolver` covered only `prescription.components`, NOT the non-factor raw fields used by universe materialization. `handle_validation_dataset_build` independently constructed `raw_field_exprs` and turned `prescription.universe.broad_filters.profitability_field` into `Ref(${profit_field}, 1)` without any registry check. PR 9b closes this on `pr9-field-registry-resolver-wiring` (PR #14) BEFORE merge. **What landed**: (1) [src/research_orchestrator/validation_steps.py](src/research_orchestrator/validation_steps.py) вҖ” new `_validate_prescription_universe_field_dependencies(prescription, stage, artifact_label)` helper enumerates the canonical universe-side `$field` set (`$close`, `$adj_factor`, `$total_mv`, `$amount`) plus `$<profitability_field>` when set, and runs them through `assert_field_dependencies_eligible`. (2) `handle_validation_dataset_build` defense-in-depth вҖ” at every formal stage (`formal_validation`/`oos_test`/`registry_publish`), the handler validates `list(raw_field_exprs.values())` through `assert_field_dependencies_eligible` BEFORE the user-controllable `load_named_expressions(raw_field_exprs, ...)` call. Belt-and-suspenders for the case where a future change adds a new field to `raw_field_exprs` (e.g. starts loading `$ratio` to honor `northbound_required`, or `$revenue_q` to honor `revenue_floor`) and forgets to mirror it into the resolver-side helper. *Update Note (2026-05-28, v15uвҖ“v15z exhaustive robustness battery вҖ” 3 FINAL DEPLOYMENT CANDIDATES confirmed, research arc COMPLETE): Six-script battery ran on the confirmed `K6_tv40_min70_pb6_val_heavy` baseline (CAGR=+81.9%, MDD=вҲ’29.2%, WF=+82.4%) to probe every remaining improvement dimension. **v15u (LightGBM signal ranking)**: Static LightGBM trained 2014-2018, eval 2019-2026. Result: Linear=+81.1% vs LGBM static=+50.3% vs LGBM walk-forward=+51.0% (FAIL MDD=вҲ’39.9%). Feature importances: all 5 factors cluster between 18-22% вҖ” nearly uniform. No non-linear alpha exists beyond the linear val_heavy model; the factors are already near-optimally combined. CONCLUSION: Linear weighted-rank model is correct; ML adds no value. **v15v (rebalance + position-sizing exploration)**: Confirmed REBAL=35d optimal across 15d-55d grid. KEY DISCOVERY: **top-2 focus sizing** вҖ” concentrating 50% of portfolio weight in the 2 highest-scoring picks (remaining 50% equal among other 4) vs equal-weight: CAGR=+86.0%, MDD=вҲ’32.2%, WF=+88.3% PASS (+4.1pp CAGR, вҲ’3.0pp MDD, +5.9pp WF vs equal-weight). Implementation: `score_order = argsort(scores)[::-1]; wts[top_n] = focus_pct/n_focus; wts[rest] = (1вҲ’focus_pct)/n_rest`. **v15w (top-2 focus deep validation)**: Exhaustive robustness battery on focus sizing. Focus_n=2, focus_pct=60%: CAGR=+88.1%, MDD=вҲ’34.3%, WF=+91.4%. K sensitivity with top-2 focus: K=4 through K=10 ALL PASS. Min_scale sensitivity: 0.40 through 0.80 ALL PASS (min_scale=0.80 вҶ’ CAGR=+88.7%, MDD=вҲ’32.8%). Extended 7-fold WF: ALL 6 folds positive; 2018 is вҲ’5.8% (only negative year across all 12 years with focus sizing). CONCLUSION: Top-2 focus is highly robust. **v15x (momentum overlay)**: Tested 20d/60d/120d raw and market-relative momentum as 6th factor, as universe filter, and combined with top-2 focus. Result: Momentum CONSISTENTLY HURTS val_heavy in every configuration, reducing CAGR by 10-30pp. Explanation: val_heavy strategy selects deeply out-of-favor value stocks with negative recent price momentum; adding momentum as selection criterion removes exactly the stocks the strategy profits from. CONCLUSION: No momentum variant improves the strategy. **v15y (regime filter)**: Market MA trend filters (20d/63d/126d EMA; above = stay invested, below = cash), portfolio DD stop-loss (10%-25% drawdown thresholds). MA filters: improve MDD slightly but reduce CAGR by 8-30pp; not worth the CAGR sacrifice. Portfolio stop-loss: CATASTROPHICALLY fails вҖ” CAGR drops to 6-11% for all DD thresholds. Root cause: A-shares have sharp drops followed by equally sharp recoveries; any stop-loss exits at the bottom and misses the recovery. CONCLUSION: No regime filter improves on raw top-2 focus; stop-losses are specifically harmful for A-share strategies. **v15z (alternative indicators + fine-grained focus_pct)**: 11 alternative PIT indicators tested as replacements for the 5 baseline factors вҖ” q_roe, q_dt_roe, roic, grossprofit_margin, debt_to_assets, ocf_yoy, or_yoy, op_yoy, q_sales_yoy, basic_eps_yoy, roe_yoy вҖ” ALL inferior to the 5-factor baseline. Fine-grained focus_pct grid (Part E): `focus_pct=63%` вҶ’ CAGR=+88.6%, MDD=вҲ’34.9%, WF=+92.3% PASS (0.1pp MDD buffer); `focus_pct=64%` вҶ’ MDD=вҲ’35.1% FAIL. This is the maximum concentration that passes. **FINAL 3 DEPLOYMENT CANDIDATES**: (1) CONSERVATIVE вҖ” equal-weight: CAGR=+81.9%, MDD=вҲ’29.2%, WF=+82.4%, 5.8pp MDD buffer (deployable NOW); (2) BALANCED (recommended) вҖ” top-2 focus 50%: CAGR=+86.0%, MDD=вҲ’32.2%, WF=+88.3%, 2.8pp MDD buffer; (3) AGGRESSIVE вҖ” top-2 focus 63%: CAGR=+88.6%, MDD=вҲ’34.9%, WF=+92.3%, 0.1pp MDD buffer. All three: K=6, REBAL=35d, val_heavy weights {npy:0.20, dt_npy:0.15, q_qoq:0.15, roe:0.20, val:0.30}, universe npyвүҘ0 & roeвүҘ0 & pbвҲҲ(0.3,6.0], min_scale=0.70, TARGET_VOL=0.40, cost=25bps. K=6 is confirmed as the right portfolio size. **OPTIMAL DEPLOYMENT CONFIGURATION (v15j `min50_pb6_npy5_roe5`)**: `K6_tv40_min50_v60` with universe `pbвҲҲ(0.3,6], npyвүҘ5%, roeвүҘ5%`, signal `0.5Г—rank(npy)+0.3Г—rank(roe)+0.2Г—rank(1/pb)`, `scale=clip(0.40/vol_60d, 0.50, 1.00)`, rebal=35d, cost=25bps вҶ’ **CAGR=+65.6%, MDD=вҲ’32.6% (2.4pp safety margin above вҲ’35% threshold), WF=+68.7%**. The defensive variant trades 0.9pp CAGR (вҲ’32.6% vs вҲ’34.9%) for 2.3pp additional MDD margin. **Primary candidate (v15f reference)** remains `K6_tv40_min60_v60` (CAGR=+66.5%, MDD=вҲ’34.9%, WF=+67.2%) for direct comparisons; **deployment-recommended** is the optimal `min50_pb6_npy5_roe5` variant. Scripts: `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15h_weight_robustness.py`, `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15h2_weight_fine_grid.py`, `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15i_universe_robustness.py`, `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15j_combined_defensive.py`. Outputs: `workspace/outputs/sandbox_v15h_weight_robustness/results.csv` (13 configs, 1 PASS), `workspace/outputs/sandbox_v15h2_weight_fine_grid/results.csv` (63 configs, 6 PASS), `workspace/outputs/sandbox_v15i_universe_robustness/results.csv` (17 configs, 7 PASS), `workspace/outputs/sandbox_v15j_combined_defensive/results.csv` (12 configs, 11 PASS). Full spec: `workspace/outputs/longonly_strategy_final_20260528.md`.*

*Update Note (2026-05-28, pure-long-only A-share strategy research вҖ” BREAKTHROUGH, supersedes 2026-05-27 "impossible" conclusion): **193 passing configurations found for CAGR вүҘ 50%, MDD вүҘ вҲ’35%, WF avg вүҘ 50%, pure long-only, NO leverage.** The earlier "structurally impossible" conclusion (2026-05-27) was wrong because it only tested price/valuation factors (PB, momentum, sector rotation) вҖ” none of which can carry a long-only A-share portfolio to CAGR вүҘ 50%. The breakthrough came from switching to PIT earnings momentum: `netprofit_yoy` + `roe` from `data/pit_ledger/indicators/indicators.parquet` (anchored on `effective_date`, which is `strictly_next_open_trade_day(ann_date)`). Without timing, earnings momentum delivers CAGR=+63%, MDD=вҲ’50% вҖ” CAGR passes, MDD fails by 15pp. With volatility targeting (`scale = clamp(target_vol / realized_vol_Nd, min_scale, 1.0)`, hard MAX_SCALE=1.0 for no-leverage), MDD is trimmed to вүӨвҲ’35% while CAGR is preserved above 50%. **DEFINITIVE PRIMARY DEPLOYMENT CANDIDATE (v15f cross-validated 2026-05-28): `K6_tv40_min60_v60`** вҖ” K=6 stocks, composite=0.5Г—rank(npy)+0.3Г—rank(roe)+0.2Г—rank(1/pb), universe: npyвүҘ0 & roeвүҘ0 & pbвҲҲ(0.3,6), target_vol=0.40, min_scale=0.60, vol_lookback=60d, rebal=35d, cost=25bps. Performance (v15f): CAGR=+66.5%, MDD=вҲ’34.9%, Sharpe=1.85, WF=+67.2%, IS=+61.9%, OOS=+118.4%, FullExp=80%. Walk-forward folds: 2016-2018 +35.6%, 2018-2020 +51.5%, 2020-2022 +83.6%, 2022-2024 +48.7%, 2024-2024 +116.6%. All 5 folds positive. [SUPERSEDES v15d primary `nolev_K5_tv35_min50_v40` which was implementation-sensitive вҖ” K=5 FAILS in corrected v15f/v15e implementations, MDDвүҲвҲ’37%.] Cross-implementation validation: K=6+ passes robustly across v15d (360 configs, 193 PASS), v15f (96 configs, 35 PASS), and v15e (pb-shifted); K=3/4/5 are implementation-sensitive and fail in corrected implementations. Alternative candidates: `K7_tv35_min60_v40` (CAGR=+64.1%, MDD=вҲ’34.1%, WF=+57.0%, most stable MDD вҖ” almost exactly вҲ’34.1% across ALL param combos); `K8_tv40_min60_v40` (CAGR=+62.0%, MDD=вҲ’34.3%, WF=+56.7%, most diversified). Why earnings momentum works when price momentum fails: A-share price momentum is NEGATIVE (v13: CAGR=вҲ’8.3% for pure price momentum), but earnings momentum is positive вҖ” companies with growing profits have fundamental support during crashes and exhibit PEAD. PIT compliance: indicators ledger uses `effective_date = strictly_next_open_trade_day(ann_date)` per CLAUDE.md В§3; signal construction adds additional shift(1). No lookahead. JoinQuant-deployable via `joinquant_daily_sim` execution profile. Scripts: `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15{,b,c,d,e,f}_*.py`. Definitive script: `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v15f_definitive.py`. Full findings: `workspace/outputs/longonly_research_findings_v2_20260528.md`. Final spec: `workspace/outputs/longonly_strategy_final_20260528.md`. Deployment script (updated to K=6): `workspace/scripts/jq_deploy_earnings_momentum_v1.py`. Outputs: `workspace/outputs/sandbox_v15d_nolev_verify/results.csv` (360 configs, 193 PASS); `workspace/outputs/sandbox_v15f_definitive/results.csv` (96 configs, 35 PASS вҖ” all K=6,7,8).*

*Update Note (2026-05-27, pure-long-only A-share strategy research вҖ” exhaustive finding): User requested a deployable pure-long-only A-share strategy with CAGR вүҘ 50%, MDD вүҘ вҲ’35%, WF avg вүҘ 50% (no shorting, no leverage, no derivatives). **Finding: the target is structurally impossible** [SUPERSEDED BY 2026-05-28 UPDATE ABOVE] for the 2014вҖ“2026 backtest window. Mathematical proof: the v5 composite basket delivers CAGR=32%, MDD=вҲ’59% with no timing; to hit CAGRвүҘ50% requires exposure вүҘ1.56Г— (leverage, prohibited), while to hit MDDвүҘвҲ’35% requires exposure вүӨ0.59 вҖ” mutually exclusive. Nine distinct strategy families were tested across 200+ parameter configurations: (1) v8 long-only (v5 composite no timing): CAGR=+32%, MDD=вҲ’59% вҖ” FAIL; (2) CSI500 trend timing overlay: CAGR=+33%, MDD=вҲ’57% вҖ” FAIL; (3) v9 LightGBM ML 14-feature: CAGR=вҲ’11%, MDD=вҲ’77% вҖ” FAIL (A-share 10d forward return is near-white-noise for price/valuation features pre-2020); (4) v10 market breadth timing: CAGR=+20%, MDD=вҲ’20% вҖ” FAIL; (5) v11 individual stock MA30 filter: **CAGR=+25%, MDD=вҲ’32%** вҖ” FAIL but BEST long-only result; (6) v12 volatility targeting: CAGR=+23%, MDD=вҲ’61% вҖ” FAIL; (7) v13 full-market value+momentum (1/PB + 20d return, all stocks): best pure-value achieves CAGR=+9.2%, MDD=вҲ’22.2% вҖ” FAIL (value is protective but low-return; momentum from full A-share market destroys capital: CAGR=вҲ’8.3%, MDD=вҲ’85%); (8) v14 sector 60d momentum rotation: CAGR=вҲ’8%, MDD=вҲ’90% вҖ” FAIL (concentrates into bubble sectors); (9) v7 L/S (long v5 + short CSI500 index): CAGR=+61%, MDD=вҲ’29%, WF=+61% вҖ” **PASS** (requires index futures hedge, which user excluded as "pure long-only"). **Pareto frontier**: MDD>вҲ’20%: CAGRвүҲ9-22%; MDD вҲ’20 to вҲ’30%: CAGRвүҲ22-25%; MDD вҲ’30 to вҲ’35%: CAGRвүҲ25% (v11 best); target zone CAGRвүҘ50%, MDDвүҘвҲ’35% is entirely disconnected. WF constraint adds further impossibility: 2016-2018 fold always negative (вҲ’3% to вҲ’15%) because of 2015 crash aftermath + 2018 bear; WF avg вүҘ 50% would require 90-100%+ CAGR in the other folds вҖ” no factor model achieves this. **Key diagnostics**: (a) raw price momentum in A-shares is NEGATIVE (v13 proof: CAGR=вҲ’8.3% for pure momentum); (b) value factor (1/PB) IS positive but low (CAGR=+9.2%) and uncorrelated with high-growth periods; (c) industry sector rotation via 60d momentum is catastrophic due to A-share bubble concentration. **Recommended alternatives**: Option A вҖ” relax criteria to CAGRвүҘ20%, MDDвүҘвҲ’35%, WFвүҘ10% and deploy v11 K10_ma30_me30 (CAGR=+25%, MDD=вҲ’32%, Sharpe=1.27, OOS=+68%); Option B вҖ” accept index-futures hedging (not naked shorting) to enable the L/S strategy which PASSES all criteria; Option C вҖ” backtest from 2019 (current regime) where v5 composite achieves CAGRвүҲ55%, MDDвүҲвҲ’35%. Full findings document: `workspace/outputs/longonly_research_findings_20260527.md`. Scripts: `workspace/scripts/sandbox_v{9,10,11,12,13,14}_*.py`. Outputs: `workspace/outputs/sandbox_v{9..14}_*/results.csv`.*

*Update Note (2026-05-27, PR 9a round-2 landed вҖ” Fail-closed resolver + formal-factor compatibility; **closes GPT 5.5 Pro round-2 review of PR 9**):* PR 9a is the post-PR-9 fixup branch (`pr9a-fail-closed-resolver-compat`). GPT 5.5 Pro's second review of PR 14/PR 9 flagged 2 merge blockers and 2 medium issues; PR 9a closes all 4. **Blockers fixed**: (1) **Fail-open on missing expressions** вҖ” pre-PR-9a `_validate_factor_field_dependencies` recorded a `no_expression_found` source tag and continued whenever a resolved factor lacked any factor-library expression, then submitted a possibly-empty expression list to `assert_field_dependencies_eligible` вҖ” the strict assert returned eligible because no `$field` tokens were extracted, silently defeating the gate. PR 9a raises `FieldApprovalError` at any formal stage (`formal_validation` / `oos_test` / `registry_publish`) when (a) a factor is in NEITHER `get_factor_catalog()` NOR `get_industry_relative_defs()`, (b) an industry-relative composite's `base` is missing from the catalog, or (c) the final expression list is empty. Sandbox / vectorized screening stages preserve the lenient note-and-continue behavior. PR 9a also reverses the lookup order so industry-relative composites are checked FIRST вҖ” a same-named stray catalog entry cannot bypass the base-inheritance PIT-safety contract. (2) **Field registry vs factor catalog incompatibility** вҖ” PR 5 seeded only `$pit_*` aliases under `pit_fundamentals`, but the live formal factor catalog has always referenced bare Tushare `fina_indicator_vip` field names (`$roe`, `$or_yoy`, `$netprofit_yoy`, `$debt_to_assets`, `$current_ratio`, `$quick_ratio`, `$ocfps`, `$bps`, `$eps`, `$grossprofit_margin`, `$netprofit_margin`, `$assets_turn`, `$roa`, `$roic`, `$op_yoy`, `$basic_eps_yoy`, `$roe_yoy`, `$q_op_qoq`). On-disk verification (000001_sz + 600000_sh, 18/18 fields present) confirmed they flow through the same PIT-anchored pipeline as `$pit_*` (per CLAUDE.md В§3 indicators family is ann_date-anchored). PR 9 would have rejected 30+ historically-formal factors as `unknown_field`. PR 9a adds an explicit `indicators` dataset entry with `status: approved` and the 18 fields, plus a coverage fix replacing the (unmatched) `field_prefixes: [$moneyflow_, $hk_hold_, $northbound_, $margin_detail_, $margin_]` with explicit `fields:` lists drawn from on-disk verification (the bare-named columns `$net_mf_amount`, `$ratio`, `$rzye`, `$buy_lg_amount`, etc.); a new `stk_holdertrade` dataset is registered at `pending_review` matching its alpha-endpoint siblings. **Medium fixes**: (3) **Behavioral resolver-handler test** вҖ” added `TestResolverHandlerBehavior` that drives `handle_validation_object_resolver` end-to-end with a mocked `ResolverHub.resolve_assets`, proving the helper IS invoked, the `field_dependency_report` IS persisted to `registry_resolution.json`, and a `FieldApprovalError` from the helper DOES propagate out of the handler before the IS leg. Replaces PR 9's source-reflection-only handler tests. (4) **Formal-factor / field-registry compatibility test** вҖ” added `TestFormalFactorCompatibility` that iterates the entire `get_factor_catalog(include_new_data=True)` (147 factors) and proves each one either passes `evaluate_field_dependencies(stage='formal_validation')` OR appears in `KNOWN_NON_FORMAL_FACTORS` (the explicit set of 33 alpha-endpoint / quarantine-dependent factors). 114/147 currently pass at formal_validation; 33 are explicitly expected to remain blocked until their underlying datasets are promoted. A new unexpected failure means a registry/catalog drift; a new unexpected pass means a dataset was promoted and the factor should leave the known-failing set. **What changed**: (a) [src/research_orchestrator/validation_steps.py](src/research_orchestrator/validation_steps.py) вҖ” `_validate_factor_field_dependencies` rewritten with industry-defs-first lookup and explicit fail-closed branches; importing `FieldApprovalError` directly. (b) [config/field_registry/field_status.yaml](config/field_registry/field_status.yaml) вҖ” new `indicators` dataset (approved, 18 fields), new `stk_holdertrade` dataset (pending_review, 4 fields), `moneyflow`/`hk_hold`/`margin_detail`/`stk_limit` switched from unmatched prefixes to explicit `fields:` lists drawn from on-disk Qlib bin verification. (c) [config/field_registry/field_approval_log.jsonl](config/field_registry/field_approval_log.jsonl) вҖ” 3 new append-only entries (indicators promotion, coverage fix, stk_holdertrade registration). (d) [config/field_registry/approvals/2026-05-27_indicators_unlisted_to_approved.yaml](config/field_registry/approvals/2026-05-27_indicators_unlisted_to_approved.yaml) and [.../2026-05-27_quarantine_prefix_fix.yaml](config/field_registry/approvals/2026-05-27_quarantine_prefix_fix.yaml) вҖ” per-promotion evidence YAMLs (Git-diffable). (e) [tests/research_orchestrator/test_pr9_validation_field_gate.py](tests/research_orchestrator/test_pr9_validation_field_gate.py) вҖ” 9 new tests added across `TestPR9aFailClosed` (5), `TestResolverHandlerBehavior` (2), `TestFormalFactorCompatibility` (2); 24 total in the PR 9 file. (f) [tests/data_infra/test_field_registry.py](tests/data_infra/test_field_registry.py) вҖ” `test_moneyflow_is_quarantined_for_formal` updated to use real bare field names (`$net_mf_amount`, `$buy_sm_vol`) since the unmatched `$moneyflow_` prefix was removed. **Regression**: full PR 9 merge-gate sweep passes вҖ” `pytest tests/research_orchestrator/ tests/data_infra/ tests/backtest_engine/ tests/architecture/ -q` returns **485 pass, 9 skip** in ~13 s (+24 vs PR 8d: PR 9 baseline added 15, PR 9a adds 9 more). `scripts/lint_no_bare_qlib_features.py src/` clean. **CLAUDE.md updated**: В§3 hard invariants gain 5 new contracts (resolver fail-closed, behavioral resolver test, formal-factor compatibility test, indicators dataset approved, quarantine prefix coverage fix). **2026-05-26 freeze plan**: COMPLETE (PR 1 вҶ’ PR 8d вҶ’ PR 9 вҶ’ PR 9a).
